# Progress

[2026-05-27] Moved the "Delete room" affordance out of the switcher dropdown and into the Edit dialog. Switcher entry renamed from "Customize this room…" to **Edit room** (locale `rooms:customizeRoom` value updated; key kept to avoid churn across 39 locales) and the modal heading changed from "Customize room" to "Edit room" (`rooms:editTitle`). The top-level "Delete room…" menu item is gone; `RoomEditDialog` gained `onRequestDelete?` + `canDelete?` props and renders a destructive "Delete room…" button at the bottom-left of the footer (trash icon, `text-destructive` hover, disabled with the `deleteLastRoomDisabledHint` tooltip when only one room remains). The switcher wires the prop: clicking Delete inside Edit closes the edit dialog and opens the slug-typed `RoomDeleteConfirm` — so the dangerous step is still one extra click behind the confirm, just no longer a peer of the switch list. Verified in-browser: dropdown shows {Cabinet Room, bla, Open in new window, Edit room, Add room…} (no top-level Delete), clicking Edit room opens "Edit room" dialog with the new Delete button in the footer, clicking it transitions cleanly into the existing confirm with the slug gate.

[2026-05-27] Implemented all three follow-ups from `docs/ROOMS_WORKSPACES_PRD.md` §10 (the rooms regressions reported the same day). **§10.1 Stale list.** Extended `useRoomsStore` (`src/stores/rooms-store.ts`) with debounced refetch on `window.focus` + `visibilitychange→visible`; added a `BroadcastChannel('cabinet-rooms')` pub/sub (`src/lib/cabinets/rooms-events.ts`) so multi-window/multi-tab mutations propagate instantly; the switcher now refetches `/api/rooms` (with `cache: "no-store"`) every time its dropdown opens. `resolveDefaultRoom` self-heals `data/.home/home.json` when `defaultRoom`/`lastActiveRoom` point at a dead slug — verified: the live `home.json` was rewritten from the dead `hilss-home` to `Cabinet` on first GET. **§10.2 Edit reliability.** `updateRoomMeta` now writes atomically (`.tmp-<pid>-<ts>` + rename); the edit dialog no longer self-closes on success (parent owns the close+invalidation), stays open with an inline error on PATCH failure, and shows a "Folder name on disk stays as X" hint distinguishing display name from slug; the switcher's `handleRoomSaved` busts `invalidateCabinetOverview(path)` and the `cabinet.name.<path>` localStorage cache, reloads the tree, and broadcasts so peer windows refresh. Verified end-to-end in-browser: rename → switcher trigger updated to "Cabinet Room (renamed)" immediately, disk manifest atomically updated; reverted via API and dropdown picked up the rename on next open. **§10.3 Delete room.** New `deleteRoom()` in `src/lib/cabinets/rooms.ts` and `DELETE /api/rooms` (accepts `?path=` or body `path`): moves the room dir to `data/.trash/<slug>-<ISO-ts>/` (soft delete, reversible by hand), repoints `home.json` if the deleted slug was `defaultRoom`/`lastActiveRoom`, and returns the trash path. Refuses: the home container (`.`), non-direct children of `DATA_DIR` (traversal), a path with no `.cabinet`, and the last remaining room — all four guards verified live (400 each). New `room-delete-confirm.tsx` is a GitHub-style confirmation: warning list, recovery note, slug-typed gate (button disabled until the user types the directory slug), inline error stays open on failure. New switcher entry "Delete room…" in the customize area (destructive styling, disabled when only one room remains). On success the switcher snaps to the new default room before the refresh lands so the user never renders a now-missing path; tree-store/editor-store selections cleared; overview cache + name localStorage busted; rooms-store + tree reloaded; broadcast emitted. Locale strings added under `rooms:*` in `src/i18n/locales/en.json` (en only; `scripts/i18n-translate.mjs` propagates to the other 38 locales later). tsc + eslint clean. End-to-end browser verification: switcher dropdown refetches on open (confirmed by mutating via curl while the dropdown was closed and seeing the new state on reopen), customize dialog opens with slug hint, save propagates immediately, delete confirm enforces slug typing, full delete→trash→restore round trip preserved a multi-MB room intact.

[2026-05-27] Consolidated the rooms docs into a single source of truth at `docs/ROOMS_WORKSPACES_PRD.md` (the former `docs/ROOMS_V3_TRUE_ISOLATION_PLAN.md` is now a one-line stub redirect). Added a "Known gaps & follow-ups (2026-05-27)" section to the PRD covering three regressions reported against the shipped switcher: (1) the room list goes stale relative to disk because `useRoomsStore.load()` early-returns once `loaded === true` and the switcher only force-refreshes after in-app Add/Edit dialogs — observed showing `Cabinet` + `bla` while disk also held `temp` (real room) and `hilss-home` (folder without `.cabinet` but pointed to by `home.json` `defaultRoom`); fix is refresh-on-open + visibility/focus refetch + cross-window `rooms:invalidated` (Electron IPC + `BroadcastChannel`) + heal `home.json` when `defaultRoom` is dead. (2) Room-name edits don't reliably reflect everywhere — `RoomEditDialog` writes manifest `name` (not the slug, on purpose) but the drawer/header subscribe via tree-store/app-store paths that hold cached names, so the visible name lags until reload; also no atomic write and the dialog can hide PATCH failures. (3) No delete-room affordance — users drop to `rm -rf`, leaving dangling refs in `home.json` and the search DB; design specifies a `DELETE /api/rooms` that moves the dir to `data/.trash/<slug>-<timestamp>/`, closes the DB handle, repoints `home.json`, emits `rooms:invalidated`, with a slug-typed confirm in the per-room Customize menu (not top-level) and guards against deleting the home or a room open in another window. Filed three TaskCreate entries (#1 stale list, #2 edit reliability, #3 delete-room). No code changes; docs + task list only.

[2026-05-22] Wrote `docs/DICTATION_PRD.md` — full PRD for offline voice dictation via whisper.cpp. Mic button on the shared composer (chat + task + replies) and the Tiptap `.md` editor; click-to-toggle with a right-click/long-press helper menu; first-use explainer popup + Settings → Dictation section. Engine is `smart-whisper` (whisper.cpp) run in an Electron `utilityProcess`, exposed over `window.CabinetDesktop.dictation.*`; renderer captures 16kHz mono PCM via AudioWorklet (no ffmpeg) and inserts text at the caret. On-device/free/private; one-time ~142MB model download to userData. NOT a wrapper around OS dictation (no API to start it). Phase 0 is a signing/entitlements de-risk spike before any UI (same hardened-runtime area as the v0.4.x DMG breakage). No code yet — doc only.

[2026-05-22] Moved agent-picking from onboarding to the agents page. (1) Onboarding "Build your team" step (`TeamBuildStep`) stripped to title + Back/Next only ("for now"); removed the department-column picker, drag-to-scroll machinery, phase animation, and all picker props (parent now passes just onBack/onNext). The mandatory-agent set still seeds the launch payload, so a default team is still created. Leaves a few unused onboarding helpers/parent locals as lint warnings (matches the pre-existing baseline; picker may return). (2) Agents page `/#/agents` "Add an agent" popup (the ACTIVE one is `src/components/agents/v2/new-agent-dialog.tsx`, not the legacy `agents-workspace.tsx`) restyled to match the onboarding picker: kept the search box, group results into vertical department sections of compact checkbox rows (checkbox + emoji + name + role), multi-select with a "(N selected)" title counter, already-on-team agents disabled with an "Added" badge, and a single "Add N agents" footer button that POSTs each `/api/agents/library/<slug>/add` (409 = success) then refreshes + closes (no longer navigates to a single agent). `agents-workspace-v2.tsx` now passes `existingSlugs` to the dialog. (3) Fixed the sidebar/tree "New Agent" button: it dispatches `cabinet:open-add-agent`, but the only listener lived in the legacy workspace (not rendered by V2) — added a listener in V2's `Dialogs` that opens the dialog. tsc + lint clean. NOTE: working tree also contains unrelated in-progress work by the user (tasks board, sidebar file dialogs, new API routes) — left untouched.

[2026-05-21] Onboarding provider step polish (round 2). Dropped the harsh accent border on the selected provider row (now always `WEB.borderLight`); selection is communicated by the warm background + a soft `${WEB.accent}14` shadow ring, with a slightly stronger `${WEB.accent}1F` ring when a row's guide is open. Clicking a ready row while a guide is open now also swaps the guide to that row, so users can browse guides by clicking through the list. Guide chevron switched from `ChevronDown` (rotated 180 on expand) to `ChevronRight` with `rtl:rotate-180`, since the guide opens to the end side and the down-arrow no longer matched. The chevron + label color shifts to accent when expanded. Restyled the "More AIs" toggle as a quiet uppercase label matching "COMING SOON" (no rounded background). Moved the "Coming soon" providers (Anthropic API / OpenAI API / Google AI API / Plugin SDK) INSIDE the "More AIs" reveal, rendered as full-width rows with reduced opacity so they share the same visual rhythm as the rest of the list. Re-check providers is now a quiet text link with a small RefreshCw icon at the bottom of the list, instead of a rounded pill.

[2026-05-21] Onboarding provider step rework. Renamed heading "Agent Provider" -> "Connect your AI" and subtitle "Cabinet needs an AI CLI to power your agents." -> "Pick an AI assistant to power your agents." (English in en.json only; re-run scripts/i18n-translate.mjs to push to 39 locales). Replaced the 4-column card grid with a single-column row list inside a max-w-3xl container. Names + versions no longer truncate. Added a two-tier model: tier 1 (gemini-cli, claude-code, opencode, codex-cli) always visible; tier 2 (cursor-cli, copilot-cli, grok-cli, pi, generic) hidden behind a "More AIs" toggle. Clicking Guide on a row collapses the list to ~42% width on md+ and slides a guide column in from the end side (right in LTR, left in RTL) using a new onboarding-guide-slide-in keyframe driven by --guide-slide-from. Below md the list hides and the guide takes full width. Cursor not-detected bug is NOT addressed by this PR; separate investigation needed.

[2026-05-21] Welcome-screen blueprint: room labels are now i18n'd. `HomeBlueprintBackground` switched its hardcoded `OFFICE/STUDY/LAB/LIBRARY/KITCHEN/FAMILY/DINING/STUDIO` to `t("onboarding:blueprint.rooms.<id>")` with `text-transform: uppercase` so the blueprint look stays for Latin scripts and degrades to natural case for CJK/RTL. Added the 8 keys to `en.json` and ran `scripts/i18n-translate.mjs --all`; Gemini translated those plus any other missing strings across all 39 locales (one locale, Hausa, ended up with 2 unrelated keys as English fallback after 4 retries — both pre-existing strings, not the new room labels). Note: a couple of locales have soft ambiguities (Spanish "Estudio" covers both study + studio; Hebrew "לימוד" reads as "learning" rather than "study room"). Re-run the script per-locale to refine, or hand-edit.

[2026-05-20] Onboarding intro screen trim: shortened all three dictionary definitions in `IntroStep` (cupboard/politics/software), reworded the politics one to "Senior advisors consulting on government policy." to prime the AI-agents metaphor, and compressed the staggered reveal from ~4.2s to ~1.6s (per-element fade 0.6s → 0.4s). [2026-05-19] Documented the update-vs-release mechanism diagnosis in `docs/deployment-packaging-versioning.md` (new "Known Gaps" section + corrected the Electron-updates note). Findings: in-app update dialog isn't gated by `installKind` so `electron-macos` users get a dead source-managed modal; `hasPersistentUpdateState` (driven by the native updater's shared `update-status.json`, incl. `failed` from incomplete macOS signing) force-reopens it; "Later" dismissal is lost because it's in origin-scoped localStorage and the runtime port isn't stable. Release side: `release.yml` publishes the manifest to a `draft` release and the Electron build is a separate manual workflow, so `cabinet-release.json` can advertise a version with no installable build. Listed the UX + CI fixes needed; no code changes yet.

[2026-05-07] Expanded `docs/PROVIDER-CLI.md` §13 "Adding a new provider" from a 5-step bullet to a complete touch-list — added the previously undocumented edits (`legacy-ids.ts`, `status-bar.tsx` PROVIDER_INSTALL_URLS, test files) and an explicit "do not enumerate providers in components" note. Surfaces that read `/api/agents/providers` (Settings, composer picker, onboarding grid, providers-demo) are called out as automatic.

[2026-04-28] **Skills**: browse skills.sh, attach per agent, or `@`-mention per task. Bundles are mounted into Claude via `--plugin-dir` so they register as proper plugin skills (not just `--add-dir` files); continuation turns re-merge the mount so mid-conversation `@`-mentions take effect on the next reply. **API Keys**: a `.cabinet.env` file at the project root, edited from a preset-driven UI (OpenAI, Anthropic, GitHub, Google AI, plus Custom). Values masked as `••••<last4>`, file written `0600`, gitignored. Spawn-time merge into `withAdapterRuntimeEnv` and the PTY manager forwards keys to every CLI, so skills like `imagegen` read `OPENAI_API_KEY` without a restart. Cabinet backups gained two opt-in toggles for the same files, both defaulting off.

[2026-04-24] Perf round 2 — deeper caching + SSE consolidation + code-splitting. New `src/lib/cache/ttl-cache.ts` (generic TTL + single-flight dedupe). Wrapped four server hotspots: `readCabinetOverview` (3s TTL), `buildTree` (5s), `listAllPersonas` (5s), `discoverCabinetPaths` (10s). Result: `/api/tree` 1623ms → 8ms warm, `/api/cabinets/overview` 1067ms → 4ms warm. `listPersonas` also parallelized (Promise.all over candidates). `/api/agents/events` SSE tick: Slack channels now fetched in parallel (was 5 sequential `getMessages` calls), duplicate per-channel fetch removed, goal reads parallelized. Consolidated the dual `/api/agents/events` SSE subscription — `app-shell.tsx` now runs the single EventSource and re-dispatches `cabinet:agents/<event>` CustomEvents; `mission-control.tsx` listens to those window events instead of opening its own stream. `recent-tasks.tsx` conversation-events handler now debounced at 200ms. Code-split eight section components via `next/dynamic` in `app-shell.tsx` (AgentsWorkspace, AgentDetailV2, TasksBoard, TaskConversationPage, SettingsPage, CabinetView, RegistryBrowser, OnboardingWizard). EmojiPicker lazy-loaded through `next/dynamic` in `slash-commands.tsx` (defers `@emoji-mart/data`). Replaced `lowlight` `common` preset with a 13-language curated set in `extensions.ts`. Status-bar health poll now visibility-aware. LCP 1596 → 1515 ms (dev); prod bundle win should be bigger given the section dynamic imports.

[2026-04-24] Perf pass driven by Chrome DevTools trace. Three fixes: (1) `applyTheme()` now loads only the active theme's Google Font families instead of 30+ at once (LCP 3686ms → 1596ms). (2) New `fetchCabinetOverviewClient` dedupes in-flight requests and caches for 3s; six callers (tree-view, home-screen, ai-panel, use-board-data, agents-workspace, cabinet-view) migrated; tree-view's 5s poll now pauses when tab is hidden — initial overview calls dropped 5 → 2. (3) All eight provider `healthCheck` callsites migrated from `execSync` to new `execCli` spawn-based helper so Promise.all actually parallelizes; `/api/agents/providers` gained a 15s in-memory cache + in-flight dedupe (2200ms cold → ~5ms warm).

[2026-04-24] DATA slide cleanup: removed mouse cursor travel animation (only the click ripple remains, delay reduced to 1400ms); reverted copy column to original fade-up animations (no typewriter, no grid-collapse state); moved Night market.mp4 scene to position 0 (removed the Phuket sunset.jpg scene); removed PhotoViewer and unused typewriter code. Also fixed blank DATA slide caused by React StrictMode double-invocation: `introRan.current` guard was set to true on the first effect run, the cleanup cleared the interval, and the second run bailed out — so typing never started. Removed the guard; the effect now resets all three state vars at the top of each run so StrictMode's second invocation starts cleanly from zero. Also moved the setTimeout handles (t1, t2) to outer-scope `let` variables so the cleanup function can clear them correctly.

[2026-04-24] Added typewriter-then-slide-right intro to the DATA slide. On first mount, the copy column (badge + h2 + p1 + p2) now types in character-by-character at 6ms/char while the grid is collapsed to "0px 0px 1fr" so column 3 fills the full slide width and the text appears centered via mx-auto. The accent color on "single source", the @ glyph, and the "same files" bold all render correctly during typing. After ~2s the typing completes, then a 200ms pause triggers the CSS grid transition (column-gap and grid-template-columns both animated at 460ms ease) that reveals columns 1 and 2 — the text naturally slides right as the left columns expand. Sidebar rows and the viewer panel use animationPlayState:"paused" while hidden and flip to "running" when showSidebar becomes true (simultaneously with the grid expansion), so the staggered row fade-ins and cursor animation all play relative to when the sidebar first appears rather than component mount.

[2026-04-24] Rebuilt the Data slide's left column as an auto-rotating showcase of five knowledge-base scenes to demonstrate the breadth of file types Cabinet supports — the old single static tree of file icons didn't convey that web apps, linked repos, office docs, and media types are all first-class. New `SCENES` array in `slide-data.tsx` cycles every 3800ms through: (1) **Thailand Trip** — itinerary markdown, photos, video, spreadsheet budget, audio notes, flight PDF; (2) **Tax 2026** — a live Calculator web app embedded inside the folder alongside income sheet, receipts PDF, deductions note, W-2, CPA notes docx; (3) **Health** — vitamins CSV, supplements markdown, dosage xlsx, lab results PDF, progress chart image; (4) **Work** — Q2 report PDF, client contract PDF, board deck pptx, revenue xlsx, policy docx, all-hands notes; (5) **cabinet-repo** — README, package.json, src folder, schema.ts, .repo.yaml — a linked Git repo as a first-class tree node. Each scene has a one-line caption below the sidebar that reads as the "why" of that file arrangement (e.g. "Tax 2026 — a live calculator web app, embedded right in your cabinet"). Scene dots under the caption show position in the rotation. Adopted the vivid icon palette from the `Supported File Types` table in `data/getting-started/index.md`: a constant `ICON` object maps gray/green/red/violet/pink/cyan/amber/blue/orange to Tailwind-500 hex values so markdown is gray, CSVs/xlsx/apps are green, PDFs are red, videos cyan, audio amber, code violet, docx blue, pptx orange, Git branches orange, images pink — each file type announces its shape at a glance instead of everything reading as a uniform mocha blur. Rotation logic uses a local `intervalId` captured in the `useEffect` closure (previous attempt leaked through a window-scoped handle and got re-fired across HMR remounts, causing the carousel to advance 3× faster than intended). Tree root row and child rows each animate in with staggered `cabinet-tour-fade-up`; the whole tree container is keyed on `scene.id` so React remounts it on each swap and the row-by-row stagger replays cleanly per scene. The `@Market Research` floating chip from the previous Data slide was removed — the rotating scenes + captions carry the "all kinds of content" story more effectively than a one-off mention demo. Left column also got a bit wider (`minmax(280px, 340px)`) to give the tree room for longer filenames like `Chiang Mai temple.jpg`.

[2026-04-24] Redesigned the tour's intro slide around a staged expansion animation and restored the sidebar's yellow-amber accent on the Cabinet chrome. Removed the "WELCOME" chip and the "All ▾" badge from `slide-intro.tsx` — the copy now opens directly with "Meet your Cabinet." + "Your AI team. Your knowledge base. One place." and the Cabinet header pill no longer carries a trailing depth-chip it never actually needed. The intro cabinet now starts narrow (92px wide) with opacity 0, fades in as a tight near-square, then expands horizontally to the tour's 300px width over 680ms via a CSS `transition: width` with a `cubic-bezier(0.22, 1, 0.36, 1)` (subtle overshoot ease-out). After the expansion settles, the "Cabinet" title text fades in inside the header (new `titleDelay` prop on `MockupSidebar` drives the delayed `cabinet-tour-fade-up` animation on the title span), then the DATA / AGENTS / TASKS tab buttons pop in one by one staggered 180ms apart (the existing `tabsPopIn` got a new `tabsPopInDelay` prop so the intro can retime the baseline away from its default 900ms). [2026-04-23] Removed legacy `/jobs` page and pruned the sidebar footer. The bottom icon row in `src/components/sidebar/sidebar.tsx` used to carry Home / Jobs / Settings; the first two were redundant (Home is already the "cabinet" wordmark in the header, and the Jobs button routed to the pre-agents JobsManager at `#/cabinet/./jobs`, which is no longer part of the system) so the footer is now just Settings. Ripped out the supporting route plumbing as well: deleted `src/components/jobs/jobs-manager.tsx` and the whole `src/components/jobs/` folder, removed the `JobsManager` import + `section.type === "jobs"` branch in `app-shell.tsx`, dropped `"jobs"` from `SectionType` in `app-store.ts`, stripped the `jobs` hash build/parse branches (including the bare `/#/jobs` alias) in `use-hash-route.ts`, and removed the `jobs` case in `return-to-chip.tsx`. Cabinet-view's "jobs" count pill and tasks-board schedule view still reference the scheduled-jobs domain concept (per-agent cron jobs) — that's a separate surface and was intentionally left alone.

[2026-04-23] Onboarding lands on Kanban with clean filters. `usePersistentState` in `tasks-board-v2.tsx` already defaulted to `"kanban"` (good), but first-time users who went through onboarding in a prior build could carry in stale `cabinet.tasks.v2.view = "list"` or `cabinet.tasks.v2.trigger = "heartbeat"` and end up on an unfamiliar view with filters active (the original UX-audit #51 foot-gun). `handleWizardComplete` in `app-shell.tsx` now writes `"kanban"` to `cabinet.tasks.v2.view`, `"all"` to `cabinet.tasks.v2.trigger`, and removes `cabinet.tasks.v2.agent` so a freshly onboarded user always lands on the Kanban board with no filters — no stale state can leak through.

[2026-04-23] Tasks board skeleton loader. Replaced the bare `Loader2` spinner on the Tasks board with view-aware skeletons so the page feels responsive from the first paint instead of looking "stuck at 0 of 0 tasks" for the 1–2 s while `/api/agents/conversations` loads (this is what the user was seeing when they reported `/#/cabinet/./tasks` "doesn't show"). New `src/components/tasks/board-v2/board-skeletons.tsx` exports `KanbanSkeleton` (5 lane columns with 2–3 placeholder cards each, matching the real lane titles), `ListSkeleton` (10 varied-width rows with alternating background stripes), and `ScheduleSkeleton` (6 agent rows with timeline segment bars), plus a `BoardSkeleton` dispatcher that renders the right one based on `view`. Each placeholder is a `bg-muted/60 animate-pulse` bar; `aria-busy="true"` + `aria-label="Loading tasks"` on the container for screen readers.

[2026-04-23] Drawer animation polish. (1) Reordered the drawer tabs from Agents · Tasks · Data to **Data · Agents · Tasks** so the most-used surface leads. (2) Tasks drawer rows now fade-in + slide-in-from-top with the same 22 ms stagger the Agents drawer uses; capped at 12 rows so long task lists settle quickly. (3) Data drawer tree now has a flowing waterfall stagger — `TreeNode` gained an optional `animationDelayMs` prop that the parent threads into children with `+30 ms` per descent level and `+14 ms` per sibling (capped at 360 ms). Top-level tree rows get `index * 22 ms`, so nested files inherit and extend the cascade. Result: when the Data drawer opens, every visible row (regardless of depth — already-expanded subtrees included) ripples in from top to bottom like a drawer being pulled out. Touched: `src/components/sidebar/tree-view.tsx`, `src/components/sidebar/tree-node.tsx`, `src/components/sidebar/recent-tasks.tsx`.

[2026-04-23] Sidebar drawer redesign — replaced the three-section vertical accordion (AGENTS / TASKS / DATA) with a horizontal "physical cabinet drawers" tab row. The sidebar now shows a 3-column tab strip in a pill container; exactly one drawer is open at a time, matching the metaphor the user asked for (each drawer = one mini portal). Active tab lifts slightly with a soft shadow + ring; inactive tabs are muted and flat. Clicking a drawer tab (a) opens that drawer inside the sidebar AND (b) routes main to the corresponding section: Agents → agents workspace, Tasks → tasks board, Data → home/page. Drawer content animates with `fade-in slide-in-from-top-1 duration-200 ease-out`; agent rows stagger 20 ms apart for a drawer-pull feel. `activeDrawer` is auto-synced with `section.type` (so hash-nav or Cmd+K jumps flip the sidebar too) and persisted under `cabinet.sidebar.drawer`. Per-drawer Plus action surfaces on hover over the active tab (add-agent / add-task / add-page) so the icons from the old per-section headers aren't lost. The Data drawer preserves the KB context menu (Add Sub Page / Load Knowledge / Copy Full Path / Open in Finder) via right-click on the drawer content. Removed the short-lived TopNav I shipped earlier today (its role is now owned by the drawers); moved Home + Jobs icon buttons into the sidebar footer next to the existing Settings gear and New Page / New Cabinet pair. Touched: `src/components/sidebar/tree-view.tsx`, `src/components/sidebar/sidebar.tsx`, `src/components/layout/app-shell.tsx` (TopNav removed), deleted `src/components/layout/top-nav.tsx`.

[2026-04-23] Added `data/architecture.md` — a KB page with four Mermaid diagrams documenting Cabinet's architecture: high-level components (Next.js app / daemon / data / AI providers), AI task/conversation sequence (structured adapter vs terminal/PTY), storage model (/data layout + API routes), and the runtime split between the Next.js app (4000) and cabinet-daemon (4100). Includes a summary of the key architectural rules the diagrams encode.

[2026-04-23] Pre-Release final tranche — cleared 5 more P0s (#2, #3, #7, #14, #16) plus partial #10. (1) **#3 hash-route aliases** — `parseHash()` in `use-hash-route.ts` now recognizes bare `/#/agents`, `/#/agents/<slug>`, `/#/tasks`, `/#/tasks/<id>`, `/#/jobs` and resolves them to the root cabinet, so every shared link of those shapes renders the right view instead of silently redirecting to Home. (2) **#7 task detail timeout** — `task-conversation-page.tsx` gains an 8 s connect watchdog: if the initial `fetchTask(taskId)` hasn't resolved, the status pill flips `connecting → unreachable`, the heading drops the literal "Loading…" in favor of the prompt first line or a real message, and a **Retry** button appears that increments a `retryNonce` and re-runs the fetch. Error path now also flips the pill to "error" with the same Retry button. (3) **#2 tasks board 0-tasks recovery** — header count now uses `filteredTasks.length` whenever *any* filter is active (was only for agent filter, hiding the trigger-filter-hides-everything case). Added an amber "N tasks hidden by filters · Clear filters" banner in the board body when `tasks.length > 0 && filteredTasks.length === 0`, so a stale `cabinet.tasks.v2.trigger` value in localStorage can no longer silently wipe the board. (4) **#14 API dedup** — new `src/lib/api/dedup-fetch.ts`: in-flight-request deduper (plus optional short-TTL cache) that collapses identical concurrent GETs to one network request. Wired at the hot first-paint call sites: `use-provider-icons.ts`, `app-store.loadProviders`, `app-shell.tsx` config fetch, `cabinet-view.tsx` config fetch, `mission-control.tsx` config fetch, `status-bar.tsx` (both health endpoints + providers/status), `data-dir-cache.ts` health fetch, `use-cabinet-update.ts` system/update fetch. The audit's `providers ×3 / overview ×5 / health ×3` burst now collapses to one request each. (5) **#16 top-nav IA** — new `src/components/layout/top-nav.tsx`: a 40 px header row mounted above `<main>` in AppShell with Home / Agents / Tasks / Jobs / Settings tabs (icon + label, or icon-only below `sm`), aria-selected wired to the current section, click routes via `setSection()` using the current cabinet scope. Includes a mobile-only hamburger at the left that toggles `sidebarCollapsed` so the existing mobile slide-in sidebar has a visible entry point (partial #10). (6) **#10 mobile MVP** — partial: hamburger in TopNav + responsive label hiding at `<sm`. Status-bar horizontal-overflow polish and mobile editor toolbar deferred. (7) **#13 fonts** — still blocked on the ongoing theme-initializer WIP; no edits to that file. Touched: `use-hash-route.ts`, `task-conversation-page.tsx`, `tasks-board-v2.tsx`, new `api/dedup-fetch.ts`, `use-provider-icons.ts`, `app-store.ts`, `app-shell.tsx`, `cabinet-view.tsx`, `mission-control.tsx`, `status-bar.tsx`, `data-dir-cache.ts`, `use-cabinet-update.ts`, new `layout/top-nav.tsx`.

[2026-04-23] Added `data/experiments/` section with five interactive physics simulations, each a self-contained embedded app (index.html + `.app` marker) using vanilla JS + Canvas 2D: **double-slit** (photon-by-photon buildup of Fraunhofer fringes with wavelength/slit-width/separation controls), **pendulum-wave** (N tuned harmonic oscillators producing phase-locked patterns over an adjustable cycle period), **projectile-motion** (ballistics with angle/velocity/gravity/height/drag plus trajectory trails and drag-free comparison), **wave-interference** (two coherent point sources with draggable positions, ripple and time-averaged-intensity modes, adjustable phase/wavelength/damping), and **brachistochrone** (race between line/arc/cycloid/parabola paths solving ∫ds/v with cycloid winning via calculus-of-variations fit). Also wrote `experiments/index.md` indexing the section.

[2026-04-23] Audited all 112 avatars under `public/agent-avatars/` and fixed three classes of bugs. (1) Six avatars had `fill="undefined"` from a generator bug and failed to render — gave each a sensible background (`avatar-86/93/94/98/107/108`; `94` also had undefined face/skin fills). (2) Fifteen avatars with the long-hair tombstone path (`M34 70 … Z`) had hair completely covering the face (03, 12, 19, 21, 30, 53, 59, 65, 67, 69, 70, 71, 96, 99, 105) — rewrote the hair path to use `fill-rule="evenodd"` with an inner circle subpath (r=20 @ 60,54) so hair now frames the face instead of covering it. Harry-Potter-style glasses on avatar-19 are now visible, Che's beret on 21 sits above a visible face, Gandalf's beard on 65 shows, etc. (3) Three avatars with bun/bun-buns used the thin crescent fringe (`M40 50 Q60 34 80 50 Q80 44 60 38 Q40 44 40 50 Z`) as their only hair, which rendered as a ribbon across the forehead (04, 17, 74) — replaced with a fuller dome fringe path (`M38 52 Q38 28 60 26 Q82 28 82 52 Q78 42 60 42 Q42 42 38 52 Z`) that reaches above the top of the face circle and covers the forehead. Verified all 112 via Chrome headless render.

(1) **#18 alert/confirm** — new toast helper at `src/lib/ui/toast.ts` (`showError / showSuccess / showInfo / showToast`) dispatching the existing `cabinet:toast` event picked up by `SystemToasts`, plus a promise-based `confirmDialog({ title, message, confirmText, destructive })` at `src/lib/ui/confirm.ts` backed by a new `ConfirmDialogHost` component mounted in AppShell (base-UI `Dialog`, destructive variant, dismiss-on-backdrop, autofocus on confirm). Migrated 10 `alert()` + 4 `window.confirm()` call sites across `settings-page.tsx`, `agent-detail-v2.tsx`, `version-history.tsx`, `task-conversation-page.tsx`, `edit-user-avatar-dialog.tsx`, `edit-agent-identity-dialog.tsx`, and `onboarding-wizard.tsx`. (2) **#8 agent Recent work fragments** — `normalizeSingleArtifactCandidate()` in `conversation-store.ts` now requires every artifact-path candidate to either contain a directory separator or end in a known file extension, AND to have no whitespace in the path-head segment. [2026-04-23] Shipped Issue #1 of the Pre-Release tracker: world-class search palette. New daemon module under `server/search/` builds a `flexsearch` Document index over `/data/**/*.md` on daemon boot (plaintext via `src/lib/markdown/to-plaintext.ts` + gray-matter frontmatter), serves ranked results via `GET /daemon/search?q=&scope=&limit=`, and incrementally re-indexes on `chokidar` add/change/unlink (debounced 150 ms) — broadcasts `search:indexed` on the existing WS event bus. `src/app/api/search/route.ts` now proxies to the daemon and degrades to a structured 503 with a "start the daemon" hint instead of spinning forever (UX audit #110). Replaced the old `SearchDialog` with a VS Code-style 2-pane `SearchPalette` (`src/components/search/search-palette.tsx`): scope tabs (All / Pages / Agents / Tasks), match-count chips, grouped results by kind, right-pane snippets with line numbers and `<mark>`-highlighted matches, recent-queries / recent-pages empty state, and a one-click "Ask the cabinet" fallback (via the existing headless agent endpoint) on zero results. New `src/hooks/use-global-hotkeys.ts` is now the single document-level listener: `Cmd+K` opens the palette from anywhere (including inside the Tiptap editor — link shortcut rebound to `Cmd+E`), `/` opens it when focus is idle (not inside an input, contenteditable, ProseMirror, or xterm), and the prior `Cmd+S / Cmd+\` / Cmd+Shift+A / Cmd+M / Cmd+Shift+.` bindings are consolidated here. Also shipped the new `data/getting-started/PRE-RELEASE-ISSUES/` page tracking all 19 P0 findings from the UX audit. Verified live: `?q=dumbledore` returns results in 1 ms against the in-memory index, watcher picks up file adds and unlinks within ~1 s. Deleted `src/components/search/search-dialog.tsx` and `src/components/shortcuts/keyboard-shortcuts.tsx` (fully superseded).

[2026-04-22] Follow-up fixes for the manual terminal persistence flow, found via end-to-end testing with 4 providers (claude/codex/opencode/gemini). Two leaks were silently force-finalizing manual Claude sessions after ~10s: (1) the daemon's `/session/:id/output` poll-completion shortcut called `completeClaudeSession` on idle detection — now guarded with `active.trigger !== "manual"`; (2) `maybeResolveCompletedConversation` in `conversation-store.ts` flipped `meta.status` to `completed` on any detail-fetch that saw `transcriptShowsCompletedRun` return true — now short-circuits when `meta.trigger === "manual"` and `meta.status === "running"`. Also tuned the awaiting-input oscillation: Claude's idle prompt continuously re-renders, which was firing `scheduleClaudeBusyFlip` within 400ms and flickering the chip; busy-flip now requires 2s sustained AND ≥120 bytes of new output since the snapshot (strictly longer than the 1.2s idle-flip window). Verified: manual Claude stays live with `status=running, awaitingInput=true` stable, daemon `exited=false` throughout idle, graceful Done closes to `completed` in ~4s. One-shot providers (codex/opencode/gemini) naturally exit after their prompt completes (unchanged — they don't have an idle prompt to stay at).

[2026-04-22] Manual terminal-mode tasks now stay alive on idle instead of force-exiting ~1.2s after Claude's TUI settles at its `>` prompt. When the CLI goes idle on a manual run the daemon flips `meta.awaitingInput = true` (status chip turns amber "awaiting input") and keeps the PTY alive; when new output streams in after the user types into the xterm, it flips back to false. Scheduled jobs / heartbeats / agent-triggered runs keep the classic auto-exit so they don't accumulate unclosed sessions. New graceful close path: a green "Done" button appears in the terminal-mode header for manual running/awaiting tasks, wired to a new `action: "close"` on `PATCH /api/agents/conversations/[id]` → `POST /session/:id/close` → `pty.write("/exit")` + 2s SIGTERM fallback. The natural PTY exit then finalizes as `status: "completed"`, distinct from Stop (SIGTERM + failed). Users can also type `/exit` or Ctrl+D directly in the xterm — that always worked, we just stopped force-exiting on top of it. Threaded `trigger` through `PtySession` / `SpawnPtyInput` / `createSession`; both WS-connect and `POST /sessions` daemon paths now read `meta.trigger` before spawn. `finalizeConversation` clears `meta.awaitingInput` on terminal statuses so exited sessions don't stay "awaiting-input" in the UI. Touched: `server/pty/types.ts`, `server/pty/manager.ts`, `server/pty/claude-lifecycle.ts`, `server/cabinet-daemon.ts`, `src/lib/agents/daemon-client.ts`, `src/lib/agents/conversation-store.ts`, `src/app/api/agents/conversations/[id]/route.ts`, `src/components/tasks/board-v2/board-actions.ts`, `src/components/tasks/conversation/task-conversation-page.tsx`.

[2026-04-22] Overhauled the post-exit UX for terminal-mode tasks. (1) Terminal-mode tasks now auto-switch from Terminal to Details tab the moment the PTY exits — the raw xterm replay of a claude-code TUI session was unreadable (hundreds of duplicate "thinking with xhigh effort" spinner frames once ANSI positioning was stripped). (2) When the user does click back to Terminal after exit, they get a new `TerminalExitedView` (`src/components/terminal/terminal-exited-view.tsx`) with a clean status header (exit cleanly / failed / errorKind+Hint banner), a run-length-compressed transcript tail (spinner redraws collapse to one line × N), and a "Show raw replay" escape hatch that mounts the classic `WebTerminal`. (3) Fixed upstream transcript corruption: `stripAnsi` / `stripAnsiText` now catch DEC-style single-char ESC sequences (`\x1B7`, `\x1B8`, `\x1Bc`, `\x1B=`, etc.) that were leaking into `meta.summary` as literal "78─────" garbage, plus charset-designate two-byte sequences. Also changed `completeClaudeSession` and the poll-based `/session/:id/output` finalize path to feed `finalizeConversation` a distilled one-liner instead of the full TUI-noise transcript, and taught `finalizeConversation` to preserve stream-extracted `meta.summary`/`artifactPaths` when the finalize-time parse comes back empty (was clobbering clean values with prompt-echo fragments). Touched: `src/components/tasks/conversation/task-conversation-page.tsx`, `src/components/terminal/terminal-exited-view.tsx` (new), `src/lib/agents/conversation-store.ts`, `server/pty/ansi.ts`, `server/pty/claude-lifecycle.ts`, `server/cabinet-daemon.ts`.

[2026-04-22] Quieted "xterm.js: Parsing error: {}" console spam in `src/components/terminal/web-terminal.tsx`. xterm's VT parser calls `logService.error(...)` at `error` level whenever it recovers from an unknown CSI/DCS escape state — which some CLIs (codex, claude-code) emit routinely during status redraws. The error is non-fatal (parser returns to idle and keeps going) but clutters DevTools. Set `logLevel: "off"` on the Terminal constructor. Also hardened `writeToTerminal` / `ws.onmessage` to drop zero-length chunks and ignore unexpected WebSocket payload types (Blob etc.) — defensive against future sources of the same log.

[2026-04-22] Fixed stale-content flash when opening a markdown artifact from a conversation transcript. Root cause: `loadPage()` in `src/stores/editor-store.ts` only wrote state asynchronously (after `fetchPage` resolved), while `setSection` + `focusPath` in `openArtifactPath` fired synchronously — so `KBEditor` re-rendered with the previous file's content for the duration of the fetch. Fix: `editor-store.ts` now synchronously clears `content` and sets a new `isLoading` flag when navigating to a different path, plus a race guard (`get().currentPath !== path → return`) on each post-fetch `set` so a slow earlier fetch can't clobber a newer navigation. `src/components/editor/editor.tsx` now tracks a `renderedPath` local state (flipped inside the existing content-setter effect) and paints a blurred-background + spinner overlay over the Tiptap area whenever `isLoading || renderedPath !== currentPath` — covering both the fetch window and the async `markdownToHtml` → Tiptap sync window. Wrapped the scroll container in a `relative` parent so the overlay sits in the viewport instead of the scrollable content. Same-path reopens stay instant via the existing `kb-page-cache` fast path.

[2026-04-22] Sped up terminal-task first paint per `data/PRDs/terminal-task-first-paint.md`. `src/components/terminal/web-terminal.tsx` now kicks off `/api/daemon/auth` + the PTY WebSocket in parallel with the xterm dynamic imports and buffers incoming bytes until the terminal finishes constructing (flushed FIFO on mount). Added `webpackPrefetch: true` magic comments on the five xterm imports so idle browsers prefetch them. `src/components/tasks/conversation/task-conversation-page.tsx` now reads an `earlyIsTerminal` hint from a new client-side cache (`src/lib/agents/terminal-mode-cache.ts`, populated by every consumer of `conversationMetaToTaskMeta`) and mounts the xterm shell before the full task detail fetch resolves. Browser-verified: WS+bytes arrive within ~1.6s on warm dev nav and buffer safely for 60s+ while xterm compiles on cold nav, flushing instantly when the terminal is ready. Non-terminal (structured) task view is unchanged.

[2026-04-22] Added `data/PRDs/terminal-task-first-paint.md` — PRD for fixing the 4–16 second delay before PTY output renders in terminal-mode tasks. Chrome DevTools timing pins the dominant cause to `WebTerminal` awaiting 5 serial dynamic xterm imports (2.6s warm / 8.5s cold) before opening the daemon WebSocket; secondary cause is `TaskConversationPage` gating render on the full `fetchTask` which is queued behind ~20 parallel app-shell API calls. PRD proposes (A) connect WS in parallel with imports + buffer-and-flush, (B) optimistic terminal-shell mount from the already-fetched conversations list.

[2026-04-22] Fixed "Conversation not found" 404 when deleting tasks (e.g. a heartbeat in the "Your Turn" column) whose `meta.json` carried a stale `cabinetPath` from an older migration (e.g. `jobs/career-ops` while the file actually lives under `data/career-ops/...`). [2026-04-22] Deduped the cabinet overview agents list by slug, nearest-cabinet wins. If the user wants to see a sub-cabinet's own editor, they navigate into that cabinet. [2026-04-22] Fixed duplicate React key warning on `/cabinet/./agents`. `agents-workspace.tsx` had five places (`key={agent.slug}`) inside `agents.map(...)`, but when the +2 visibility mode surfaces both a cabinet-owned `editor` and an inherited `editor` from a sub-cabinet, two items share the slug and collide. Switched all five to `agent.scopedId ?? (agent.cabinetPath ? \`${agent.cabinetPath}::${agent.slug}\` : agent.slug)`, matching the existing pattern at line 2090. Verified via DevTools — the two "Encountered two children with the same key, `editor`" errors are gone.

[2026-04-22] Fixed a runaway request storm on app load. `NewCabinetDialog` is rendered once per tree node inside `tree-node.tsx`, and its `NewCabinetOverlay` was mounted unconditionally — so `useAgentPicker()` fired `GET /api/agents/library` on every tree node (observed ~250+ in-flight requests per page load with 65 cabinets × StrictMode double-mount). Fix gates the overlay on `open` in both controlled and uncontrolled branches of `src/components/sidebar/new-cabinet-dialog.tsx`, so the fetch only runs when the user actually opens the dialog. Verified via Chrome DevTools: requests dropped from 283 (252 pending `/api/agents/library`) to 26 with zero library fetches on idle.

[2026-04-22] Docs follow-up for the PTY extraction. `README.md` architecture tree now lists `server/pty/` alongside `server/cabinet-daemon.ts`. `PRD.md` daemon-composition block replaces the old "Terminal Server ← existing PTY/WebSocket" line with a `PTY module` entry pointing at `server/pty/`, plus structured adapters, scheduler, event bus, and the actual HTTP/WS endpoint list. [2026-04-22] Killed the standalone terminal server and extracted the PTY layer out of the daemon. Deleted `server/terminal-server.ts` (it was a strict subset of the daemon with zero client coupling and no auth — a security footgun waiting to happen). Pulled the PTY-specific helpers out of `server/cabinet-daemon.ts` (2029 → 1570 LOC) into a new `server/pty/` module: `ansi.ts` (`stripAnsi`, now shared between PTY and structured finalizers), `types.ts` (`BaseSession`, `PtySession`, `CompletedOutputEntry`), `claude-lifecycle.ts` (`claudePromptReady`, `submitInitialPrompt` with the 600ms paste-window guard, `completeClaudeSession`, `maybeAutoExitClaudeSession`, `consumeStructuredOutput`/`flushStructuredOutput`, `distillPtyOutput`, `scheduleStreamCabinetExtraction`), and `manager.ts` (the `createPtyManager` factory exposing `spawn` + `writeInput`; deps-injected so it stays decoupled from conversation-store and event-bus callbacks). The daemon keeps the unified `sessions` map (PTY + structured) and delegates PTY spawn via `ptyManager.spawn`, stdin injection via `ptyManager.writeInput`. Swapped `scripts/dev-daemon.mjs` to spawn tsx in `watch --clear-screen=false` mode so PTY-module edits hot-restart the daemon (verified: touching `server/pty/manager.ts` increments the "Cabinet Daemon running" line in the log). Removed `dev:terminal` from `package.json`, purged `server/terminal-server.ts` from `scripts/prepare-electron-package.mjs` (replaced with `server/pty`), updated `CLAUDE.md` (rule #8 + commands table + architecture layout), and refreshed `data/getting-started/architecture.mermaid` to show the PTY module as a sub-graph inside the daemon instead of a dashed-alt node.

[2026-04-22] Fixed three gaps in multi-task dispatch inheritance surfaced by a live Harry Potter fan-out test. (1) `resolveDispatchRuntime` (`src/lib/agents/action-dispatcher.ts`) now pushes the parent conversation's provider + adapterType + model + effort to spawned sub-tasks by default, falling back to the target persona's declaration only when the parent has none. Action-authored `providerId`/`adapterType`/`model`/`effort` on a `LAUNCH_TASK` still win. Effort is portable across providers via a new `providerSupportsEffort()` helper in `provider-registry.ts`. `LaunchTaskAction`/`ScheduleJobAction`/`ScheduleTaskAction` in `src/types/actions.ts` gained optional `providerId`/`adapterType`. `action-parser.ts` picks up the new fields from JSON + inline forms; `action-validator.ts` adds `provider_unavailable` (hard) and `cross_provider_push` (soft) warnings; the dispatcher system prompt in `conversation-runner.ts` now explains inheritance so the LLM stops clobbering user intent. (2) Codex error surfacing: `codex-stream.ts` now handles in-stream `{"type":"error"}` and `{"type":"turn.failed"}` events and writes the unwrapped inner message to `CodexStreamAccumulator.errorMessage`; `codex-local.ts` prefers that over filtered stderr and adds a `classifyCodexModelUnavailable` matcher. `cabinet-daemon.ts` now passes `result.errorMessage` to `classifyError` when stderr is empty. A new `ConversationErrorKind` variant `model_unavailable` lights up the UI with a "pick a different model or switch to API-key auth" hint instead of the previous empty-transcript "unknown" shrug. (3) Codex model catalog refresh: `codex-cli.ts` gained `gpt-5.4` (the only model that works on ChatGPT-plan Codex accounts) and annotated `gpt-5.2-codex`, `gpt-5.1-codex-max`, `o3`, `o4-mini`, `gpt-4.1*` with `requires: "api_key"`; `ProviderModel.requires` is exposed through `/api/agents/providers` and rendered as an "API key" badge in `task-runtime-picker.tsx`. Verified end-to-end: re-ran the parent → 5-child fan-out with `claude-code/opus/medium` and all 5 children now inherit that runtime (previously every child fell back to `codex-cli` with empty adapterConfig); fired an unsupported-model run and confirmed `errorKind: model_unavailable` + the real codex reason make it to `meta.errorHint`. New unit tests: `action-dispatcher.test.ts` (6 cases covering same-provider inheritance, parent-provider push, action override, effort portability, effort-not-supported drop, persona fallback); `codex-local.test.ts` gains a `{type:error}` fixture that asserts the inner-message unwrap + classifier match.

[2026-04-22] Agent color now applies even when an avatar image is set. `AgentAvatar` tints the image-wrapper background with the agent's color (explicit hex via `tintFromHex`, or slug-derived via `getAgentColor`) instead of `bg-muted`, giving a colored halo through rounded corners / transparent PNGs. `AgentPill` likewise paints the pill background with the agent tint when an avatar image is present, so board pills carry the identity color whether the agent uses an icon or a photo.

[2026-04-22] Fixed Claude Code terminal-mode tasks sitting at the prompt waiting for a manual Enter. `submitInitialPrompt` (and the `/session/:id/input` continue path) wrote `\r` only 150 ms after the prompt text, inside Claude's TUI paste-detection window — so the Enter was absorbed into the `[Pasted text #N +X lines]` block instead of submitting. Bumped the delay to 600 ms so the paste window closes before Enter arrives.

The button is destructive-styled, only renders when `filteredTasks.length > 0`, and routes through the existing `ConfirmPopover` with an explicit count + "can't be undone" warning. [2026-04-21] First-turn blank-gap fix on new conversations. `readTurn1` in `conversation-store.ts` now synthesizes a pending agent turn 1 with `content: "Working on it…"` when `meta.status === "running"` and the transcript is empty, matching what continue turns already do via `continueConversationRun`. Error paths (failed/cancelled/completed-with-empty-output) still return `null` so real failures aren't masked. `waitForConversationCompletion` in `conversation-runner.ts` now polls the daemon immediately (first poll at t=0 instead of after a 700 ms sleep) and uses a 250 ms interval for the first 5 s before backing off to the existing 700 ms. Together these cut ~500–700 ms off the perceived blank gap between "prompt sent" and "agent responding" on a cold start, and replace the silent window with a visible "Working on it…" placeholder.

[2026-04-21] Conversation side panels (board-v2 `DetailPanel` and global `TaskDetailPanel`) can now go fullscreen via a new Maximize2/Minimize2 toggle in the panel header. The panel swaps from its 420–460 px side-panel positioning to `fixed inset-0 z-50` when enlarged; clicking the button again (or pressing Escape on the board panel) shrinks it back. State lives in `useAppStore.taskPanelFullscreen` and auto-resets on section changes and when the panel is closed/opened, so navigating away never leaves a stale fullscreen hanging around. Board context (selected card, scroll) is preserved under the overlay, unlike the existing ↗ route-based escape hatch.

[2026-04-21] Simpler tooltip on the **Can dispatch** / **No dispatch** pill in the agent detail header. Plain-English phrasing ("Can hand off work to teammates. You approve each handoff before it runs.") plus a 5-way fan-out example ("Try: 'Launch 5 research tasks — one per top competitor — each on its own task.'") that mirrors how users actually phrase these prompts, and a trailing "Click to turn off" line in the on-state. No jargon like LAUNCH_TASK.

[2026-04-21] Tasks board agents filter now honors the cabinet-visibility toggle. `use-board-data.ts` was sending `visibilityMode=` to `/api/cabinets/overview`, but the route reads `visibility=` — so the toggle was a silent no-op and the board was pinned to the active cabinet's own agents no matter what. Changed the overview call's query param to `visibility`. Left the conversations call alone: `/api/agents/conversations` actually does read `visibilityMode`, so the two endpoints remain inconsistent with each other but both are now correctly addressed.

[2026-04-21] Fix task composer agent dropdown selection: switched `DropdownMenuItem` from `onSelect` to `onClick`. Base-ui's `Menu.Item` doesn't wire `onSelect` to clicks, so agent picks were silently dropped; matches the pattern already used in `reassign-menu.tsx` and `cabinet-task-composer.tsx`.

[2026-04-21] Task composer agent dropdown (`new-task-dialog.tsx`) now renders the real `AgentAvatar` shared component in both the trigger button and each menu item, replacing the raw emoji span. Shows uploaded avatar images when set, and falls back to the tinted icon when none — matching how the sidebar and reassign menu already render agents.

[2026-04-21] Extracted `ConversationApprovalPanel` (`src/components/agents/conversation-approval-panel.tsx`) as the single shared entrypoint for the dispatch-approval UI. Wraps `PendingActionsPanel` with the null/empty guard and an `onApproved` callback, accepts any meta shape with `id`, `cabinetPath`, `pendingActions`, `dispatchedActions` (both `ConversationMeta` and `TaskMeta` satisfy it). All three conversation views now mount it — `conversation-result-view.tsx`, `conversation-live-view.tsx`, and `task-conversation-page.tsx` — and each carries a sibling-view comment above the render so a future change here automatically propagates (or at minimum leaves a breadcrumb). The mistake this fixes: I added the raw panel to two of the three views and missed the task-viewer page because its render site lives in a different component tree.

The app includes a `.app` marker, voltage-adjustable capacitor field, animated charged oil droplets with gravity/electric-force balance, selectable drops, force bars, balance voltage controls, and a measured-charge readout that infers `q = mg/E` and quantizes it to nearest multiples of elementary charge `e`.

[2026-04-21] Conversation turn blocks now show the actual agent's avatar + color instead of a generic sparkles circle with the label "Agent". `TurnBlock` accepts an optional `agent` prop (`AgentAvatarInput & { name? }`); `TaskConversationPage` fetches the persona from `/api/agents/personas/:slug` once per task and passes it down. [2026-04-21] Four follow-up fixes to the agent-to-agent dispatch flow so the approval panel actually works end-to-end in the task viewer. (1) Prompt: `buildCabinetEpilogueInstructions` is now async and injects the real teammate roster (slug — name — role) from `listPersonas(cabinetPath)` so agents don't hallucinate slugs; picks a generalist fallback (preference: `editor` → slug/role match of editor|generalist|assistant|copywriter|writer → any teammate) and tells the agent to route there rather than refusing when no specialist fits. Updated all five call sites to pass `cabinetPath` + `selfSlug`. (2) Finalization: removed the `if (!meta.actionsProposedAt)` guard in `finalizeConversation` that was dropping every proposal emitted on turn 2+ (when the user redirected mid-run). Now re-parses every finalize and dedupes against pending+dispatched by fingerprint. (3) Task viewer panel: `TaskMeta` carries `pendingActions`/`dispatchedActions`; `conversationMetaToTaskMeta` copies them; `task-conversation-page.tsx` renders `PendingActionsPanel` between the last turn and the composer with an `onRefresh` that re-runs `fetchTask`. Before, the panel only existed in `/#/agents/...` routes — the `/#/cabinet/./tasks/...` route (which is where the "Open in task viewer" button lands) had no panel at all, so proposed actions were invisible. (4) Session view: wired `onRefresh` through `conversation-session-view.tsx` (via a `refetchRef` + `refreshDetail` callback) to both `ConversationResultView` and `ConversationLiveView`, so approve/reject clicks actually update the panel. Verified end-to-end via Chrome DevTools: approving 2 rows spawned 2 child conversations with `trigger: "agent"` + `parentTaskId` linkage, and the panel re-rendered to show "18 pending · 2 dispatched".

[2026-04-21] Fixed the pending-actions panel so it doesn't vanish mid-run and so approve/reject actually updates the UI. Two changes to `conversation-session-view.tsx`: (1) exposed a `refreshDetail` callback backed by a `refetchRef` so both child views can re-fetch `ConversationDetail` on demand; (2) pass `onRefresh` to both `ConversationLiveView` and `ConversationResultView`. Added the `PendingActionsPanel` render to `conversation-live-view.tsx` so proposals stay visible during follow-up turns (when status flips back to `running`). Before: result view had no `onRefresh` prop wired up (so approve clicks worked server-side but the panel kept showing stale rows), and live view never rendered the panel at all (so the 10 pending tasks "vanished" the moment the user typed a follow-up).

[2026-04-21] Taught the dispatch prompt to pick a generalist fallback instead of refusing. When `canDispatch` is on, `buildCabinetEpilogueInstructions` now picks a fallback agent from the roster (preference: `editor` → first teammate whose slug/role matches editor|generalist|assistant|copywriter|writer → any teammate) and tells the agent: "If no teammate is a clear specialist fit, dispatch to the generalist `<slug>` rather than refusing. Mention in your reply that you routed to the generalist so the human can reassign if they want." This stops the CEO from pausing with an ask_user when there's no dedicated agent — it routes to editor/copywriter and tells you, so you can reassign in one click instead of restarting the turn.

[2026-04-21] Fixed a second dispatch bug where actions emitted on follow-up turns were silently dropped. `finalizeConversation` was gating the whole proposal path on `if (!meta.actionsProposedAt)` — an idempotency flag set after turn 1 — so when the user redirected mid-run ("send to copywriter") and the CEO emitted a fresh `cabinet-actions` block on resume, the parser never looked at that turn's output. Removed the guard; now every finalize re-parses and dedupes new proposals against `meta.pendingActions` + `meta.dispatchedActions` by fingerprint. Exported `fingerprint` from `action-parser.ts` for the dedupe check.

[2026-04-21] Fixed dispatch hallucination: `buildCabinetEpilogueInstructions` now fetches `listPersonas(cabinetPath)` and injects the real teammate roster (slug — name — role) into the prompt whenever `canDispatch` is on, plus a one-line rule "Only dispatch to slugs listed above. Do not invent slugs." Made the helper async and updated all five call sites (manual, editor, scheduled-job, resume, replay) to pass `cabinetPath` + `selfSlug`. Root cause of the 10-task Disney run that stuck: CEO proposed `cv-tailor` / `CV-tailor` but the root cabinet has an empty `cv-tailor/` dir (no `persona.md`); the persona only exists in `career-ops/.agents/cv-tailor/`, so validation correctly flagged all 10 as `unknown_agent` hard blocks. With the roster now in the prompt, agents will only dispatch to real teammates.

[2026-04-20] **PendingActionsPanel: one-click Approve all / Reject all / Deselect all.** Previously fan-outs of 500+ tasks required two clicks (Select all → Approve). [2026-04-20] **Agent-to-agent task injection with human approval.** Agents can now propose work for other agents via provider-agnostic text markers parsed from the transcript at finalization. Three action types: `LAUNCH_TASK` (immediate), `SCHEDULE_JOB` (recurring cron), `SCHEDULE_TASK` (one-shot at ISO datetime — implemented as a `oneShot: true` JobConfig that the daemon auto-disables after first fire). Both inline one-liners inside the existing ```cabinet block and a new ```cabinet-actions JSON block are supported (JSON authoritative, deduped by `type:agent:title:prompt`). Proposals are *not* auto-dispatched — they land in `meta.pendingActions` on the parent ConversationMeta and surface in a new `PendingActionsPanel` inside `ConversationResultView` for the human to bulk approve / reject. Supports 1000+ rows (cap-visible at 100, "show more" to expand). New per-persona `canDispatch` flag (defaults `true` for `type: "lead"`, `false` otherwise) gates both the system-prompt instructions (appended in `buildCabinetEpilogueInstructions`) and the dispatcher; exposed as a "Can assign tasks to other team members" toggle in the agent detail overflow menu. Validator computes soft warnings (self-dispatch, cycle risk, depth ≥ 3, inactive target, budget low) and hard blocks (unknown agent, persona cannot dispatch, invalid cron/ISO) — hard blocks disable the approve checkbox. New API: `POST /api/agents/conversations/:id/actions {approve, reject}` dispatches via in-process `startConversationRun` / `saveAgentJob` → `reloadDaemonSchedules`; writes audit into `meta.dispatchedActions` with deep links to spawned conversations/jobs; publishes `task.updated` SSE. New files: `src/types/actions.ts`, `src/lib/agents/action-parser.ts` / `action-validator.ts` / `action-dispatcher.ts`, `src/components/agents/pending-actions-panel.tsx`, `src/app/api/agents/conversations/[id]/actions/route.ts`, plus a full PRD at `data/PRDs/agent-task-injection.md`. Extended `ConversationTrigger` / `TaskTrigger` with `"agent"`, `ConversationMeta` with lineage (`parentTaskId`, `triggeringAgent`, `spawnDepth`) + `pendingActions` + `dispatchedActions`, `JobConfig` with `oneShot` / `runAfter` / `ownerTaskId`. `transcript-parser.ts` regex accepts the new markers and emits a new `actions` block type; `conversation-content-viewer` renders it. `npm run lint` + `npm run build` clean.

[2026-04-20] **Consolidated every heartbeat-editor dialog into shared `HeartbeatDialog`.** Complementary to yesterday's `NewRoutineDialog` consolidation. New `src/components/agents/heartbeat-dialog.tsx` owns its own state (cron + active), manages the PUT to `/api/agents/personas/<slug>` for save and `action: "run"` for run-now, and routes to the agent detail page via an `Edit agent` button in the footer. Title shows the agent's colored avatar + `HeartPulse` icon + "for <Agent> · <role>". Description explains the mental model: "A heartbeat wakes this agent on its own rhythm. Each time it fires, the agent checks in and decides what to work on — driven by its persona instructions. Set how often it should wake up here; to change what it does each time, open the agent page." Cron picker label reinforces: "This is how often the heartbeat wakes up." Active checkbox explains: "when off, the heartbeat won't fire automatically." Accepts an optional `missedRun` prop for the amber "did not execute" banner. Three call sites migrated: `agents-workspace.tsx` (three live callsites — team-schedule `onHeartbeatClick`, Heartbeats list row click, fullscreen-schedule `onHeartbeatClick` — now all drive one unified `heartbeatDialog: { agent, initialHeartbeat, initialActive } | null` state; dead `orgChartHeartbeatDialog` JSX + old `runOrgChartHeartbeat` / `saveOrgChartHeartbeat` handlers now unreachable but left as dead code so I don't break the mode-settings fallback render), `cabinet-view.tsx` (`heartbeatDialog` state reshaped; `runDialogHeartbeat` / `saveDialogHeartbeat` deleted; leftover `Dialog` primitive imports + `SchedulePicker` + `MissedRunBanner` + `Zap` / `Save` / `HeartPulse` / `AlertTriangle` imports cleaned up), `board-v2/schedule-dialogs.tsx` (`ScheduleHeartbeatDialog` is now a thin wrapper forwarding `state` + `onClose` + `onRefresh` into `<HeartbeatDialog>` so existing board-v2 callers keep compiling). Net: another ~270 LOC removed from the three callers, one new 190 LOC shared component. `tsc --noEmit` clean on my files; `HTTP 200`.

[2026-04-20] **Extracted `NewRoutineDialog` component; agent detail page's "Add routine" now opens the same dialog.** Pulled the full-featured new-routine UI out of `agents-workspace.tsx` into a new `src/components/agents/new-routine-dialog.tsx` so it can be reused. [2026-04-20] **Fix ARTIFACT: lines with comma-separated paths being treated as a single file.** Root cause (two parts): (1) instructions in `conversation-runner.ts` and `heartbeat.ts` were ambiguous — didn't say "one ARTIFACT: line per file", so the model sometimes emitted `ARTIFACT: a.md, b.md`; (2) `normalizeArtifactPath` in `conversation-store.ts` lazy-matched `(.+?\.[A-Za-z0-9]+)(?:\s|$)`, which swallowed the whole comma-list into one path because the next token also ended in `.md`. The transcript UI (`transcript-parser.ts`) likewise rendered one badge for the whole line. Fix: (a) tightened the prompt in both runner + heartbeat; (b) replaced `normalizeArtifactPath` with exported `normalizeArtifactPaths` that splits on `,`/`;`/multi-space before normalizing each token, used by both `parseCabinetBlock` branches; (c) added the same split in `transcript-parser.ts` so the cabinet code block renders one ARTIFACT badge per file. Added two regression tests to `conversation-store-turns.test.ts` covering meta-level parsing and the split helper itself.

[2026-04-20] **New-routine dialog redesigned — agent avatar in title, bigger fonts, shared `TaskRuntimePicker` replaces Provider+Runtime selects.** Title row now shows the target agent's colored `AgentAvatar` + "New routine" / "Edit routine" at `text-[22px] font-semibold` with a subtitle "for <Agent name> · <role>" at `text-[13px]` underneath. Description rewritten in plain English: "A routine is a prompt this agent runs on a schedule. Write the prompt once, pick when it should run, and let the agent take it from there." Bumped label font to `text-[11px] font-semibold` (from `text-[10px]`), input text to `text-[14px]` (from `text-[13px]`), textarea to `text-[14px] leading-6`. Prompt height reduced to `55vh` so the right column breathes. The two side-by-side Provider + Runtime `<select>`s are replaced by a single `<TaskRuntimePicker>` — the same cross-app model picker the tasks composer uses — so provider + model + effort selection is consistent with the rest of the app. Mapping: `jobDraft.provider`/`jobDraft.adapterType` ↔ `providerId`/`adapterType`, and `jobDraft.adapterConfig.{model, effort}` ↔ `value.model`/`value.effort`. The picker's trigger is styled `h-10 w-full rounded-lg bg-muted/60` to match the other inputs. Save button label changed from "Create job" to "Create routine". Run-now / Delete action buttons bumped to `h-9 text-[12px]`. `tsc --noEmit` clean; `HTTP 200` on `/`.

[2026-04-20] **Agent detail: fix avatar editor revert after save.** Root cause: `saveFields` called `refresh()` on success, which runs 4 parallel fetches and calls `setPersona(serverData)` — this raced with and silently overwrote the optimistic update. Fix: `saveFields` now only calls `refresh()` if the PUT returns non-OK (error path revert). Upload and delete paths use a new `applyOptimistic` callback (pure `setPersona` patch, no fetch) instead of the old `onRefresh`, so the avatar state is never overwritten on success.

[2026-04-20] **Agents page: real fix — base-ui Menu.Item uses `onClick`, not `onSelect`.** Previous rAF-based defer was a red herring. The actual bug: `@base-ui/react/menu`'s `MenuItem` type has no `onSelect` prop; React was forwarding it to the rendered `<div>` where it means "text-selection event" (useless for clicks), so every agent-pick in the Add-routine / Add-scheduled-job / Configure-heartbeat dropdowns was a silent no-op. Swapped all three `onSelect={() => …}` callsites in `agents-workspace.tsx` to `onClick={…}`. Kept the `requestAnimationFrame` defer inside `openNewRoutineFor` — now correctly useful because base-ui closes the menu on click, so the dialog needs to wait one frame for focus-lock to settle before opening. Also back-fixed the same bug I introduced earlier in the cabinet-page `AgentPickerCompact` (`cabinet-task-composer.tsx` line 212). `tsc --noEmit` clean on my files (unrelated `claude-transcript-view` import failure is separate in-progress work).

[2026-04-20] **Agents page: Add routine actually opens the dialog; contextual CTAs on Routines + Heartbeats.** Two fixes on top of yesterday's rebuild. [2026-04-20] Fixed conversation-completion toasts + chimes going silent for structured-adapter runs. Root cause was cross-process: `notificationQueue` in `conversation-store.ts` is an in-memory array, and since `cabinet-daemon` runs in its own Node process, whenever the daemon won the `finalizeConversation` race (nearly always for structured adapters) the push landed in the daemon's queue, while Next.js's SSE tick kept draining an empty queue. Fix: exported `enqueueConversationNotification(notification)` from `conversation-store.ts` with identity-based dedupe (`cabinetPath::id::status` via `buildConversationNotificationIdentity`) and called it unconditionally from `waitForConversationCompletion` in `conversation-runner.ts` once the poller sees a terminal status — next to the existing Next.js-side `publishConversationEvent("task.updated")` belt-and-braces call. Same comment pattern as the task.updated fix (2026-04-18) so the intent is obvious on inspection. Dedupe means it's safe even if a future refactor accidentally calls `finalizeConversation` on the Next.js side too. Timeout branch at the bottom of the poller still pushes through `finalizeConversation`'s normal queue so nothing changes there.

[2026-04-20] **Agents workspace Schedules: big "Add routine" CTA + embedded team schedule board with fullscreen.** The Schedules section grows a top-right, prominent 10px-tall `Add routine` button with a `Clock3` icon (plus `ChevronDown`) — it's a `DropdownMenu` that lists every agent in the team; picking one opens the existing job editor (`orgChartJobDialog`) pre-seeded with `blankJobDraft(slug, defaultProvider)` and a new `newRoutineIsNew` flag. `saveOrgChartJob` now branches on `newRoutineIsNew || !draft.id`: for new routines it POSTs `/api/agents/<slug>/jobs` (matching the detail-page `addJob` handler) and splices the created job into `agentJobsMap`; for edits it keeps the existing PUT path. Cancel/close resets the flag. Below the intro copy, the Schedules section now embeds `<ScheduleView>` (the same board-v2 wrapper used by the Tasks > Schedule view) at a fixed 460px height, with a `Maximize2` button in its header that pops it into a `94vh × 96vw` Dialog with a `Minimize2` toggle. Both inline and fullscreen schedule views wire `onJobClick` to the edit dialog (resolving the full `JobConfig` by id from `agentJobsMap`), `onHeartbeatClick` to `orgChartHeartbeatDialog`, and `onConversationClick` to the existing conversation-mode switch. [2026-04-20] **Fix: `AgentDetailV2` stuck on "Loading…" for agents outside the root cabinet.** Opening `/#/cabinet/career-ops/agents/application-assistant` hung indefinitely. Root cause: `AgentDetailV2`'s `refresh()` called `/api/agents/personas/<slug>` without a `cabinetPath` query param, so `readPersona(slug, undefined)` fell back to the root cabinet and 404'd; the render then gated on `loading || !persona` and never moved past the spinner. [2026-04-20] **Stop cabinet meta-blocks leaking into KB file bodies.** Agents were occasionally writing the epilogue ` ```cabinet SUMMARY: ... ARTIFACT: ... ``` ` block into the content of `.md` files they saved (e.g., `data/have-fun/harry-potter-8.md`), instead of keeping it as a transcript-only meta-annotation. Three-part fix: (1) tightened `buildCabinetEpilogueInstructions()` in `src/lib/agents/conversation-runner.ts` — now explicitly says the block goes at the end of the chat response (text sent back to the user), NOT inside any file content, and adds a "Never write a ` ```cabinet ``` ` block inside the body of any .md file you save" rule. (2) Added `sanitizeArtifactCabinetBlocks()` in `src/lib/agents/conversation-store.ts` — regex-strips a trailing `\n*```cabinet\b[\s\S]*?\n```\s*$` fence from any `.md` artifact before it's exposed to the UI. Path-traversal guarded (`path.resolve` must stay inside `DATA_DIR`). Wired into `finalizeConversation` (first-turn, parallel with `writeConversationMeta`/`replaceConversationArtifacts`) and both continue-turn paths (`appendAgentTurn`, `updateAgentTurn`) guarded by `!pending && turn.artifacts?.length`. (3) Cleaned `data/have-fun/harry-potter-8.md` — removed the trailing cabinet block the copywriter agent had written into the story body. `tsc --noEmit` clean.

[2026-04-19] **Task viewer transcript rendering: match the /agents transcript view.** `TurnBlock` in `src/components/tasks/conversation/turn-block.tsx` now renders agent turns via `ConversationContentViewer` instead of the Markdown prose component. User turns still use `<Markdown>` (they're chat prompts), but agent output — which for PTY/heartbeat runs is raw terminal text with embedded `SUMMARY`/`ARTIFACT`/`DECISION` CABINET blocks — goes through `parseTranscript`, which preserves newlines (`whitespace-pre-wrap` + `font-mono`), recognizes diff/code fences, and renders CABINET fields as colored labeled cards. Fixes the regression where `markdownToHtml` was collapsing newlines into spaces and dropping the "result section" clarity the old `/agents` view had. Applies everywhere `TaskConversationPage` mounts (v2 board DetailPanel + standalone `/tasks/[id]`). `tsc --noEmit` clean.

[2026-04-19] **Phase 3 of Task Board v2 shipped** — destructive drops with inline confirm. `board-actions.ts` gained `stopConversation(id, cabinetPath)` (PATCH `{action:"stop"}`) and `restartConversation(id, cabinetPath)` (PATCH `{action:"restart"}`), both wrapping endpoints that already existed in `/api/agents/conversations/[id]/route.ts`. New `confirm-popover.tsx` renders a small modal-feeling card (backdrop blur, docks near bottom on mobile, center on ≥sm) with title/body/Confirm/Cancel — destructive Confirm button goes red. Mounted once in `tasks-board-v2.tsx` controlled by `pendingConfirm: PendingConfirm | null`. `kanban-view.tsx` extended `handleDragEnd` with two destructive branches: (1) source=`running` && target≠`running` → Stop confirm (body copy switches to "Stop & archive" if the target is Archive so the user knows the combined effect; on Confirm runs `stopConversation` then, if archiveAfter, `archiveConversation`; then refresh + undo toast whose `undo` calls `restoreConversation` + `restartConversation` to recover the run); (2) source=`archive` && target=`running` → Restart confirm (spawns a fresh run from the archived conversation's original prompt via `restartConversation`; runs `restoreConversation` first so the original doesn't stay archived). Esc closes the popover; clicking the backdrop dismisses. Type-check clean. Fully Phase 3 per PRD §12 — Phase 4 (People rail drop targets for agent handoff) is next.

[2026-04-19] **Phase 2 of Task Board v2 shipped** — drag-and-drop archive/restore with a 5s undo toast. Added `@dnd-kit/core` + `@dnd-kit/sortable` + `@dnd-kit/utilities` (via `--legacy-peer-deps` due to an `@emoji-mart/react` react-peer version range mismatch — not new, same issue blocks any unrelated install). `src/app/api/agents/conversations/[id]/route.ts` gained a `boardOrder?: number` field in `PatchBody` and a `typeof body.boardOrder === "number" && Number.isFinite(body.boardOrder)` guard in the updates pass; the existing `body.archived` / `body.archivedAt` field-level updates cover archive + restore without needing a new `action:` type. `src/components/tasks/board-v2/board-actions.ts` (new) wraps PATCH calls in `archiveConversation(id, cabinetPath)`, `restoreConversation(id, cabinetPath)`, and `setConversationBoardOrder(id, boardOrder, cabinetPath)`. `src/components/tasks/board-v2/undo-toast.tsx` (new) is a fixed-position `bottom-left` toast with a 5s countdown progress bar, Undo button, and X close; takes a `PendingUndo` record `{id, message, undo()}` and calls `onDismiss` when the countdown ends OR the user clicks Undo/X. `src/components/tasks/board-v2/kanban-view.tsx` rewrite: wrapped in `<DndContext sensors={[PointerSensor({distance:6})]}>`, each lane is a `<DroppableLane>` (uses `useDroppable` with id `lane:{key}`), each card is a `<SortableTaskCard>` (uses `useSortable` with id `card:{taskId}`), per-lane `<SortableContext strategy={verticalListSortingStrategy}>`. On `handleDragEnd`, resolve `sourceLane` by scanning `byLane`, resolve `targetLane` from the over id (lane prefix or card's lane), then dispatch: (a) source≠archive && target=archive → `archiveConversation` + refresh + queue undo (`restore`); (b) source=archive && target≠archive → `restoreConversation` + refresh + queue undo (`archive`); (c) everything else = no-op (Phase 2 scope). Drop target lanes show a `ring-2 ring-foreground/40` outline via `isOver`. `DragOverlay` renders a rotated card preview (`rotate-[-2deg] shadow-2xl`) while `dropAnimation={null}`. `tasks-board-v2.tsx` holds `pendingUndo: PendingUndo | null` state and passes `onUndoQueued={setPendingUndo}` + `onRefresh={refresh}` (new from hook) into `KanbanView`; `<UndoToast>` mounted at bottom-left of the board container. A11y for free: @dnd-kit's aria descriptions ("press space bar to pick up…") now appear on every sortable card. Tested end-to-end via CDP `evaluate_script` — the PATCH flow archives/restores as expected (`archivedAt` toggles between set and cleared; `200 OK`); the synthetic `drag` tool doesn't trip @dnd-kit's 6px distance activation constraint, so UI drag verification needs a real pointer. No DnD on List or Schedule views yet (Phase 2 is Kanban-only per PRD §12). Reorder-within-lane is a no-op in Phase 2 even though @dnd-kit rearranges visually on drop — persistent `boardOrder` write comes in a follow-up. Destructive drops (Stop live run, Restart from archive, Archive a running task) remain disabled until Phase 3 which adds inline confirm popovers. `npx tsc --noEmit` clean.
