[2026-04-19] Wrote `TASK_BOARD_PRD.md` at the repo root — a focused design spec for redesigning `/tasks` into an attention-first kanban of AI conversations. Five fixed columns (`Inbox → Needs Reply → Running → Just Finished → Archive (collapsed)`) derived from conversation state instead of `board.yaml`, one card per task carrying an agent pill (color + icon + name) and a status dot matching the sidebar legend, and a slide-out right-side detail panel for nested conversation runs. DnD is the control surface: drops trigger real actions via a full drop matrix (Inbox→Running = Start, Running→Archive while live = Stop+Archive with inline confirm, Archive→Running = Restart, etc.), non-destructive drops fire with a 5s Undo toast and destructive ones show an inline confirm popover. Cross-agent handoff happens by dropping a card onto a right-side **People rail** (48→220px on hover) of agent avatars — card lands in recipient's Inbox, never auto-starts, paused agents accept drops with just a badge. Spec covers card anatomy, full drop matrix, live-SSE reconciliation rules (don't yank hovered cards), keyboard DnD (Space-to-pick / arrows / Space-to-drop / Esc), data model (new `archivedAt` + `boardOrder` fields on `AgentTask`, `board.yaml` deprecation strategy with a one-time `mtime → archivedAt` migration), API additions (`archive` / `restore` / `reorder` / `reassign` task actions + `task.reordered` SSE event), a 6-phase rollout behind a `?board=v2` flag, success metrics (p50 start-time from handoff, zero accidental live-run kills), and 5 deferred open questions (density toggle, heartbeat-card collapsing, filter set, muted tasks, batch actions). Cross-references `data/getting-started/index.md` §Agents & Tasks at a Glance, `AGENT_PAGE_PRD.md` §5.3b for the Inbox wait-don't-execute invariant, and `recent-tasks.tsx` for the just-finished 1h rule to reuse.

[2026-04-19] Enriched the sidebar **task status dots** in `src/components/sidebar/recent-tasks.tsx`: running tasks now pulse in the owning agent's own color (resolved from the overview `persona.color` via `tintFromHex`, with a deterministic `getAgentColor(slug)` fallback), so you can tell at a glance *which* agent is working. Needs-reply stays amber, failed stays red, and a new derived "just finished" state flips idle/done tasks to emerald for 1 hour after `lastActivityAt` (a local `setInterval` ticks the component every minute so fresh-green fades back to muted without waiting for an SSE event). Tooltips now spell out the state in plain English (*"Write Voldemort poems — running"*, *"PR babysitter — just finished"*). Tree-view passes its existing agents fetch (`/api/cabinets/overview`) down so no extra network call is introduced. Documented the full legend in a new **Agents & Tasks at a Glance** section inside `data/getting-started/index.md` (between Content & Features and Keyboard Shortcuts): a dot-color/meaning table, the three-state agent chip, the color-discipline rule (agent color appears only on avatar + chip dot + composer focus ring + sidebar running dots), and a short note on the Inbox wait-don't-execute convention.

[2026-04-19] Added the agent page's **Inbox** section (`src/components/agents/agent-detail-v2.tsx`) — an `AgentTask` queue rendered between the composer and Conversations when the agent has pending/in-progress assignments. Hover reveals a **Start** button on pending rows without a linked conversation; clicking Start POSTs `/api/agents/conversations` with `userMessage = "${title}\n\n${description}"` + `mentionedPaths = kbRefs`, then POSTs `/api/agents/tasks {action:"update", status:"in_progress", linkedConversationId, startedAt}` per the existing endpoint contract, and routes to the new conversation. Click a row body: if `linkedConversationId` is set we open that run; else fall through to Start. [2026-04-18] Updated `TASKS_CONVERSATIONS_PRD.md` to reflect the shipped wave: G7/G8/G9/G10/G11/G12/G13/G15/G17 flipped to 🟢 with evidence pointing at the live-run verification; added §14.5 "Cross-process event bus (Next.js ↔ daemon)" as a hard contract with new entries G22 (first-turn live SSE) and G23 (sidebar tree refresh on nested agent writes), both 🟢; added invariant #11 to §1.1 codifying that UX-relevant events must be emitted from (or polled by) the Next.js process since the daemon's event bus never reaches SSE subscribers; added §13 smoke tests S11 (live first-turn stream) and S12 (tree refresh on nested writes); rewrote §14.6 implementation order into Completed / Remaining lists.

[2026-04-18] Fixed two live bugs reported against the task/conversation flow: (1) first-turn chat didn't update until F5, and (2) sidebar tree stayed stale after agents wrote KB files anywhere deeper than the data root. Root cause of (1): the daemon runs in its own Node process, so its in-process `publishConversationEvent` calls never reached Next.js SSE subscribers, and the first-turn path only flowed through the daemon (no turn.appended/turn.updated events). Fix: emit `task.updated` from the Next.js side — on `createConversation`, on terminal completion in `waitForConversationCompletion` (announcing whichever process actually finalized), and throttled (500ms) during `appendConversationTranscript`; also dropped the 3s poll in `waitForConversationCompletion` to 700ms so live transcript diffs drive a stream of `task.updated {streaming:true}` events during the run. Root cause of (2): the `/api/agents/events` SSE's tree-change detection shallow-diffed `fs.stat(DATA_DIR)` mtime + top-level entry count, so nested writes like `data/have-fun/voldemort/index.md` never tripped it. Fix: when `drainConversationNotifications` returns any completed conversation, emit a `tree_changed` with `reason:"conversation_completed"` and refresh `lastDataVersion` so the AppShell's existing `tree_changed` listener calls `loadTree()`. Verified live against fresh `dev:all`: a new first-turn conversation produced 3 SSE events on `/events` (two `streaming:true` at 5.6s/6.3s + terminal `status:completed` at 6.3s; previously zero); the task page rendered the user turn instantly and the agent response streamed in; sidebar DATA section showed `Have fun → Voldemort` and newly-created `stream-test` without any reload.

[2026-04-18] E2E verification of the G7/G8/G9/G10/G13/G15/G17 wave against a fresh `npm run dev:all` daemon on :4100 + Next.js on :4000. Found and fixed a real bug discovered during testing: the daemon's `finalizeSessionConversation` (server/cabinet-daemon.ts) finalizes the conversation before `waitForConversationCompletion` polls, so the Next.js-side finalize path never wrote tokens to `meta.tokens`. Fixed by threading `adapterUsage` + `adapterErrorKind/Hint/RetryAfterSec` directly into the daemon's own `finalizeConversation` call. Also added `classifyError` invocation to the daemon's spawn-time catch branch so `ENOENT` (CLI not installed) surfaces as `cli_not_found` instead of `unknown`. Verified live: claude-code two-turn conversation produced `meta.tokens={input:6,output:39,cache:32929,total:45}` and `session.json` with `resumeId + codecBlob + displayId: "Claude · 37c9e295"`; continue turn's `lastResumeAttempt.result = "resumed"` confirms G8 resume path actually used the rehydrated codec blob; grok-cli test produced `meta.errorKind="cli_not_found"` + UI "cli not found" chip + remediation banner + Logs tab Classified-error section; runtime switch from Opus→Haiku mid-conversation wrote `adapterConfig={model:"claude-haiku-4-5",effort:"low"}` to meta, kept `resume=resumed` on same adapter, and Haiku answered "Tokyo"; Logs tab shows 12 sequentially-numbered events (seq=1..12) confirming G17 seq persistence; session bar renders "alive · Claude · 37c9e295 · claude_local" using the codec displayId. All 7 gaps work end-to-end against real providers.

[2026-04-18] Implementation of `TASKS_CONVERSATIONS_PRD.md` gaps G7, G8, G9, G10, G13, G15, G17 — the full highest-leverage wave from §14.5. Types: extended `ConversationMeta` with `errorKind/errorHint/errorRetryAfterSec/lastResumeAttempt`, added `ConversationErrorKind` + `ConversationErrorClassification` + `ConversationResumeAttempt`, extended `SessionHandle` with `codecBlob + displayId`. Adapter contract: `AgentExecutionAdapter.classifyError` now optional on every adapter. New shared `src/lib/agents/adapters/error-classification.ts` covers CLI-not-found / auth / rate-limit / session-expired / context-exceeded / timeout / transport / unknown; each of the 8 `*-local.ts` adapters now implements `classifyError` via the shared classifier. Added `sessionCodec` to `claude-local` (resumeId) + `codex-local` (threadId); cursor/opencode/pi already had codecs. All adapters now return `sessionParams` alongside `sessionId`. Daemon (`server/cabinet-daemon.ts`): `StructuredSession` carries `adapterSessionParams + stderrBuffer + adapterErrorKind/Hint/RetryAfterSec`; `createStructuredSession` passes `ctx.sessionParams`, buffers stderr, calls `adapter.classifyError` on failure, and writes `session.json.codecBlob` via `sessionCodec.serialize` on success. `/session/:id/output` response now includes `adapterSessionParams` + `adapterErrorKind/Hint/RetryAfterSec`. `POST /sessions` accepts `adapterSessionParams`. `daemon-client.ts`: `pollDaemonSessionUntilDone` + `getDaemonSessionOutput` return the full shape. Runner (`conversation-runner.ts`): `waitForConversationCompletion` now threads `adapterUsage` → `meta.tokens` via extended `finalizeConversation` (G7); `continueConversationRun` accepts `providerId/adapterType/model/effort` per-turn override, rehydrates `session.codecBlob` via `sessionCodec.deserialize` into `ctx.sessionParams` before execute, serializes `result.sessionParams` back to `codecBlob` after success (G8), calls `adapter.classifyError` on any failed run and writes `meta.errorKind/errorHint/errorRetryAfterSec + lastResumeAttempt` (G9+G10), switches resume → replay mode when runtime changes mid-conversation. `finalizeConversation` in `conversation-store.ts` accepts `tokens + errorKind/Hint/RetryAfterSec`. `appendEventLog` now assigns monotonic per-conversation `seq` (in-memory counter, cold-started from existing line count) and returns it; publishConversationEvent threads `seq` into the bus event. New `readEventLog(id, {fromSeq})` helper. SSE route (`conversations/[id]/events`) now honors `Last-Event-ID` header + `?lastEventId=` query, replays missed events from `events.log` before subscribing to the live bus, and emits `id: <seq>` on every event (G17). `POST /[id]/continue` accepts `providerId/adapterType/model/effort` and returns canonical `{ok:false, error, errorKind}` envelope on failures. UI: `TaskComposerPanel` fully rewritten to import the shared `ComposerInput + useComposer + TaskRuntimePicker` primitives, lazy-loads the tree as mentionable items, accepts `initialRuntime` + `onSend({text, mentionedPaths, runtime})`, snaps back to conversation runtime after send (G15). `task-client.postTurn` accepts `{mentionedPaths, runtime}` and POSTs them. `TaskConversationPage` handler refactored for the new payload; header shows errorKind chip + hint when present. `tasks-board.tsx::ConversationRow` + `task-detail-panel.tsx` render `<ProviderGlyph>` using new `useProviderIcon` hook (module-level cache, one fetch across the app) and an errorKind chip when set (G13). `TaskMeta` + `conversationMetaToTaskMeta` carry the new fields through. `LogsPanel` adds a "Classified error" section + "Session" section showing codec-derived display id. Verified: `tsc --noEmit` clean, `tsx --test` 22/22 pass across conversation-store-turns + adapter + registry suites, Chrome DevTools smoke test on running server confirms runtime picker renders with provider tabs/model rows/effort radios, `POST /continue` with `{providerId,adapterType,model,effort}` returns 202, SSE route accepts `lastEventId` and emits `text/event-stream`, provider glyph renders on task cards.

New §2 Shared-Code Contract enumerates the seven shared primitives with correct file paths (`composer/composer-input`, `useComposer`, `conversation-client`, `conversation-runner`, `conversation-store`, adapter registry, `TaskConversationPage`); new §5 API Contract with full payload shapes + canonical error envelope; new §7 Adapter Contract including proposed `classifyError` + `ConversationErrorKind` taxonomy and full session codec rules; new §8.2 surface×shared-code reuse matrix; new §13 verification matrix (11 surfaces × 8 providers = 88 cells) with seven per-cell acceptance criteria + ten secondary smoke tests; Gap Register (§14) folded inline as G1–G21 with status + unblocks; Appendix A adds a step-by-step adapter-authoring cookbook for a hypothetical `foo-cli`. Diagrams, data model, and original content preserved.

[2026-04-18] Registry imports now cache the full GitHub tree response in-process (10 min TTL) so multiple back-to-back imports don't burn through the 60/hr unauthenticated API budget. On 403/429 the error message now surfaces the rate limit clearly and mentions `GITHUB_TOKEN` as the fix (5000/hr when set). Documented the optional token in `.env.example`.

[2026-04-18] Added a one-time "Cabinet is under breaking changes" warning dialog. Shown on first mount if the user hasn't acknowledged it — stored under localStorage key `cabinet.breaking-changes-warning-ack:v1`. Mounted in `AppShell` after the onboarding wizard resolves, so new users see it right after setup, and existing dev-branch users see it once on next load. Clearing the key re-triggers it.

[2026-04-18] Guarded the RegistryBrowser import dialog against double-fire. The Import button lacked a busy-state `disabled` guard, so a fast second click fired a parallel POST — the first one created the directory, the second hit the "Directory already exists" 409. Added `disabled={importing}` on both buttons, a re-entry guard at the top of `handleImport`, and a spinner on the Import button while the request is in flight.

[2026-04-18] Fixed broken registry import during onboarding. The `RegistryBrowser` detail view was hardcoded to `window.location.reload()` on successful import, which in the onboarding overlay restarted the wizard from scratch (workspace.json isn't written until launch) and left the first import stranded — the retry then hit "Directory already exists". Added an optional `onImported(template, name)` callback to `RegistryBrowser` / `DetailView`; when provided it replaces the reload. Onboarding now hands that callback through and jumps straight to the success screen. Also hardened the import path: `downloadRegistryTemplate` and the `/api/registry/import` route now rm the partial `targetDir` on any mid-flight failure so retries aren't blocked by leftover dirs.

[2026-04-17] Move feedback + EXDEV fallback: drag-drop / Move-To / reorder now surface what's happening. Tree store tracks a `movingPaths` Set — affected rows get a `Loader2` spinner, dim to 60% opacity, and become non-interactive while the PATCH is in flight. Server-side `movePage` catches `EXDEV` from `fs.rename` (cross-device, e.g. linked external cabinet on a different mount) and falls back to `fs.cp` + `fs.rm`, so dropping into a sister cabinet that's actually a symlinked external folder no longer silently fails. Errors and confirmations now flow through a new generic `SystemToasts` component (`cabinet:toast` events with `{ kind: 'info'|'success'|'error', message }`); the move flow dispatches an info toast on success ("Moved to <parent>") and an error toast carrying the server's actual error message on failure (previously only `console.error`'d). Moved item is also auto-selected after success so the user sees where it landed.

[2026-04-17] Sidebar reorder + move-to: items in a directory can now be manually ordered. New `src/lib/storage/order-store.ts` writes integer `order` (gap-of-100 with midpoint inserts and a one-time renumber when gaps close) — to `index.md`/`*.md` frontmatter for markdown-backed nodes and to a per-directory `.cabinet-order.yaml` sidecar for non-md files (PDF, CSV, image, code, etc.). `tree-builder` reads the sidecar, hides it from listings, and the sort fallback for unordered legacy items is now `Number.POSITIVE_INFINITY` (alphabetical-after-ordered). `createPage` and `movePage` assign sane defaults; the PATCH endpoint accepts `{ toParent, prevName, nextName }` so cross-dir moves and same-dir reorders share one atomic call.

[2026-04-17] Drag-and-drop in `tree-node.tsx` got drop-zone hit-testing — top 25% / middle 50% / bottom 25% for containers (top/bottom = reorder, middle = nest into), and 50/50 split for leaf files (no nest). Insertion-line indicators render at the row top/bottom in primary color; the existing ring stays for the "into" state. Drag image is a cloned, rounded ghost (8px radius, popover bg, soft shadow) attached via `setDragImage` so the dragged row doesn't read as a rectangular browser screenshot. New `MoveToDialog` (Cmd+K-style fuzzy picker over directories/cabinets) is wired to a "Move to…" context-menu item and to a `Cmd+Shift+M` shortcut on the selected node.

[2026-04-17] Calendar past-event ↔ conversation linkage, with missed-run detection. New `scheduledAt?: string` field on `ConversationMeta`: written by the daemon at scheduler-launch time (rounded to the minute — matches `ScheduleEvent.time`), threaded through `startJobConversation` / `runHeartbeat` / `createConversation` and persisted in `meta.json`. UI builds a `Map<key, ConversationMeta>` where `key = agentSlug::sourceType::jobId::minuteIso`, fetched alongside the cabinet overview. Clicking a past pill/dot now does exact key lookup (opens the real conversation), falls back to legacy ±90s fuzzy match on `startedAt` for pre-stamp data, and otherwise treats the event as "did not run": renders muted/hollow + amber warn icon, and the edit dialog shows an amber banner listing possible causes (daemon off, schedule disabled, failed-to-start). Disabled events keep their dashed-hollow treatment so the three states are visually distinct.

[2026-04-17] `RuntimeMatrixPicker` now disables provider tabs whose CLI isn't ready (not installed, not authenticated, or disabled in Settings). Follow the install guide below."). `base-ui` TabsTrigger's `disabled` prop prevents click + keyboard activation. If the currently stored selection points at an unready provider, the picker auto-focuses the first ready tab instead. Works in both surfaces: task composer (where only ready providers were already shown) and Settings default-runtime matrix (where all enabled providers are shown so users can see what's available but can only click ones that'll actually run).

[2026-04-17] Settings → Providers now reuses the task composer's runtime picker UI for default provider/model/effort selection. [2026-04-17] Added in-UI provider verification. New endpoint `POST /api/agents/providers/[id]/verify` spawns the provider's "Verify setup" command (with `ADAPTER_RUNTIME_PATH` so PATH matches real task runs), captures stdout/stderr/exitCode, and classifies the result as one of `pass | not_installed | auth_required | payment_required | quota_exceeded | other_error` via keyword heuristics ("command not found", "quota exceeded", "payment required", "not authenticated"/"401", etc). The Settings → Providers guide and the Onboarding wizard both got a "Run verify" button per provider that shows a colored status chip, highlights which step failed (step marker turns red with "!"), and exposes raw stdout/stderr on demand. Verified classification against Claude (pass), Codex (pass), Gemini (pass), OpenCode (pass), Cursor / Pi / Grok / Copilot (`not_installed` with hint "The CLI binary isn't on your PATH yet. Rerun the Install step").

[2026-04-17] Verified headless "Reply with exactly OK" across installed providers. Claude ✅ / Codex ✅ / OpenCode ✅ (after today's stdin fix). Gemini CLI 0.1.9 rejected `--output-format` as an unknown argument, so the guide's verify command was changed to `gemini -p 'Reply with exactly OK' --yolo` and the install step was pinned to `@google/gemini-cli@latest` with a note that Cabinet's Gemini adapter needs 0.14+ for stream-json output. Cursor / Pi / Grok / Copilot are not yet installed on this machine, so their verify steps are pending install.

[2026-04-17] Fixed OpenCode adapter "silent success" bug discovered when running `google/gemini-2.5-pro` without a configured provider API key: (1) prompt is now piped via stdin instead of passed as a trailing CLI arg (matches paperclip's proven invocation and avoids the first-run migration path swallowing the prompt); (2) added a stderr filter that suppresses `Performing one time database migration…` / `sqlite-migration:*` / `Database migration complete.` bootstrap noise; (3) when OpenCode exits 0 with zero assistant messages and no session id, Cabinet now synthesizes a non-zero exit with a pointed error ("…the most common cause is a missing provider API key for the requested model e.g. GOOGLE_GENERATIVE_AI_API_KEY for google/* models…"). Updated the opencode test script to consume stdin.

[2026-04-17] Added Grok CLI (`grok_local`) and GitHub Copilot CLI (`copilot_local`) as two new structured providers. Both use plain-stdout passthrough (no stream-json contract yet), expose model selection + extraArgs config, ship install guides with the headless "Verify setup" step, and auto-register alongside the existing six. Providers API now returns 8 CLI providers / 10 adapters total (including legacy). Corrected the OpenCode install command to `npm i -g opencode-ai` (the published package name) and deleted the superseded `AI-claude-editor.md` plan doc.

[2026-04-17] Added "Verify setup — Confirm headless mode works" install step to every provider (Claude, Codex, Cursor, OpenCode, Pi) matching the Gemini pattern, so users can test each CLI end-to-end with a one-shot `Reply with exactly OK` prompt before trusting it in Cabinet task runs.

[2026-04-14] Fixed task completion detection stuck on "running". Two bugs: (1) after ANSI stripping the `❯` idle prompt merged onto the same line as `⏵⏵ bypass permissions on`, so the exact-match regex `/^[❯>]$/` never matched — loosened to `/^[❯>](?:\s|$)/`; (2) Claude Code's completion timing line uses many verbs beyond "Brewed" (Sautéed, Baked, Churned, Crunched, etc.) — `isClaudeIdleTailNoise` now matches any spinner-prefixed `Verb for [time]` pattern generically instead of hardcoding individual verbs.

[2026-04-13] Created `cabinetai` CLI package — a new npm package that serves as the primary runtime CLI for Cabinet. Architecture: app installs to `~/.cabinet/app/v{version}/` (auto-downloaded on first use), cabinets are lightweight data directories anywhere on disk. Commands: `create` (scaffold .cabinet + .agents/ + .jobs/ + index.md), `run` (ensure app installed, start Next.js + daemon pointing at cabinet dir), `doctor` (health checks), `update` (download newer app version), `import` (fetch templates from hilash/cabinets registry), `list` (discover cabinets in directory tree). Built with TypeScript + esbuild + Commander.js. Refactored `create-cabinet` to thin wrapper. Updated release pipeline (release.sh, release.yml, manifest generator, .gitignore).

[2026-04-12] Multi-cabinet conversation aggregation: when viewing a cabinet with "Include children" or "Include all descendants" visibility mode, the Agents Workspace now aggregates conversations from all visible cabinet directories. The conversations API accepts a `visibilityMode` query param and uses `readCabinetOverview` to discover descendant cabinet paths, then merges and sorts conversations from all of them. AgentsWorkspace passes the current visibility mode and re-fetches when it changes.

[2026-04-12] CEO agent first heartbeat for Text Your Mom example cabinet: created company/updates page with weekly priorities, added reality check to goals (50K MAU target requires marketing activation this week), added action-by-metric table to KPIs page, and linked updates section from root index. Three priorities set: ship P1 onboarding stories, activate paused marketing cabinets, and start investigating the critical reminder timing bug.

[2026-04-12] Cabinet UI interaction layer: clicking agents in the sidebar now opens AgentsWorkspace scoped to the cabinet (passes cabinetPath through section state → app-shell → AgentsWorkspace). Agent cards in the cabinet dashboard org chart are clickable. All agent API calls (persona GET, run, toggle, jobs) pass cabinetPath for cabinet-scoped resolution. JobsManager accepts cabinetPath prop.

[2026-04-11] Daemon recursive cabinet scheduling: the daemon now discovers all `.cabinet` files recursively under DATA_DIR and schedules heartbeats and jobs for every cabinet's agents. Schedule keys are cabinet-qualified (e.g., `example-text-your-mom/marketing/tiktok::heartbeat::trend-scout`) to prevent slug collisions across cabinets. Cabinet-level `.jobs/*.yaml` with `ownerAgent` are picked up alongside legacy agent-scoped jobs. The file watcher now monitors `**/.agents/*/persona.md`, `**/.jobs/*.yaml`, and `**/.cabinet` across all depths. API endpoints accept `cabinetPath` in request body so heartbeats and jobs execute in the correct cabinet scope with the right cwd.

Created root `.cabinet` manifest and `index.md` for the root cabinet. Renamed `data/.cabinet/` (runtime config dir) to `data/.cabinet-state/` to avoid conflict with `.cabinet` manifest file.

Users choose their default provider (Claude Code or Codex CLI) and pick a model (sonnet/opus/haiku or o3/o4-mini/gpt-4.1). Selection is saved to provider settings on launch. Non-working providers show setup guides in an expandable section.

[2026-04-11] Added fallback viewer for unsupported file types. Files like .docx, .zip, .psd, .fig, .dmg etc. now appear in the sidebar (grayed out) and show a centered "Open in Finder" + "Download" view. Uses a whitelist approach — only common document, archive, and design file extensions are shown; everything else is silently skipped. Added `/api/system/reveal` endpoint for macOS Finder integration.

[2026-04-11] Added Storage tab to Settings with data directory picker. Users can view the current data dir path, browse for a new one, or type a path manually. The setting is persisted to `.cabinet-install.json` and read by `getManagedDataDir()` at startup (env var still takes priority). A restart banner shows when the path changes. Also updated the About tab to show the actual data dir path.

[2026-04-11] Added source/code viewer, image viewer, and video/audio player as first-class file viewers. Images (.png, .jpg, .gif, .webp, .svg) render centered on a dark background with download/open-in-tab. Video/audio (.mp4, .webm, .mp3, .wav) use native HTML5 players. Tree builder now classifies files by extension and shows type-specific sidebar icons. Added node_modules and other build dirs to the hidden entries filter.

[2026-04-11] Load Knowledge now creates direct symlinks (`data/my-project -> /external/path`) instead of wrapper directories with a `source` symlink inside. Metadata is stored as dotfiles (`.cabinet-meta`, `.repo.yaml`) in the target directory, while legacy `.cabinet.yaml` is still read for compatibility. Added `isLinked` flag to TreeNode for UI differentiation — linked dirs show a Link2 icon and "Unlink" instead of "Delete" in context menus. [2026-04-18] Jobs & heartbeats calendar gets a Compact ↔ Roomy density slider. Day/week views now measure their scroll container with a ResizeObserver and compute HOUR_HEIGHT dynamically: at density=0 the visible TOTAL_HOURS exactly fits the page (no scroll), each density unit adds 1px per hour row so the grid grows past the viewport and scrolls. MIN_HOUR_HEIGHT=22 keeps the grid readable on tiny screens, and the slider is hidden in month mode where density doesn't apply. Slider lives next to the day/week/month picker in tasks-board.tsx.

[2026-04-18] Refresh perf: stop blanking the app on reload. Tree and last-opened page are now cached in localStorage and painted instantly on mount, then revalidated in the background (SWR). Onboarding config check and useCabinetUpdate deferred to requestIdleCallback so they don't sit in the critical path — and the "wizard done" flag is cached so returning users skip the blocking `showWizard === null` render that was the main blank-screen culprit. Tree cache key is bucketed by showHidden.

[2026-04-18] Fix Compact slider in Jobs & heartbeats. Wrapped the base-ui Slider in an explicit `w-24` container — the Slider Root's default `data-horizontal:w-full` had higher selector specificity than our `w-24` className override, so inside a flex row the slider was collapsing/expanding unpredictably and the thumb wasn't grabbable. Wrapping gives the Root a real 96px parent to fill.

When events fall outside the visible range on visible days, a chevron strip renders above/below the time grid: "▲ N earlier · show 4 AM" / "▼ N later · show 11 PM". Click expands the range by one hour and saves the new bounds. [2026-04-19] Fix two console errors at app boot. (1) `next-themes` 0.4.6 renders an inline `<script>` inside its provider for FOUC prevention; React 19/Next 16 logs "Encountered a script tag while rendering React component". Switched `src/components/theme-provider.tsx` to load `NextThemesProvider` via `next/dynamic({ ssr: false })` — Cabinet's own `ThemeInitializer` already applies theme classes from localStorage, so the next-themes script is redundant for our custom theme system. (2) `app-shell.tsx` initialized `showWizard` from `localStorage` inside `useState(() => …)`, so the server rendered the loading branch (`null`) while the client immediately rendered the main shell (`false`) for cached users — that mismatch was the source of the `<aside>`/`text-foreground` hydration warning. Initialized `showWizard` to `null` on both server and first client render, then read localStorage in an isomorphic `useLayoutEffect` so cached users still skip the blank-screen flash without diverging from SSR HTML.

[2026-04-19] Replace `next-themes` 0.4.6 with a tiny in-tree `<ThemeProvider>` + `useTheme()` in `src/components/theme-provider.tsx`. The upstream provider always renders an inline `<script>` for FOUC prevention, and React 19 + Next 16 logs that as a `Console Error` on every render — `dynamic({ ssr: false })` did not help because the script renders on client mount too. The replacement keeps the same API surface Cabinet actually uses (`theme` / `setTheme` / `resolvedTheme`, `attribute="class"`, `defaultTheme`, `enableSystem`, `disableTransitionOnChange`, localStorage `storageKey`), reads localStorage in `useEffect` so server and first client render match, and applies `light`/`dark` to `<html class>` post-mount. Updated four call sites to import from `@/components/theme-provider` instead of `next-themes`: `editor/emoji-picker.tsx`, `layout/theme-initializer.tsx`, `layout/theme-picker.tsx`, `settings/settings-page.tsx`. `next-themes` no longer imported anywhere in `src/`.

[2026-04-20] Terminal-mode UX refinement: removed auto-exit on cabinet-block detection. Daemon still streams meta.summary / meta.artifactPaths live so the Details tab fills in as the CLI emits the epilogue block, but the PTY is left running so the user gets the full terminal experience and can continue the conversation. Task only finalizes when the user manually exits the CLI (Ctrl-D / /exit). Also deleted the redundant "Continue the conversation" composer card that used to appear under the terminal at idle — the CLI itself is the composer.

[2026-04-20] Codex terminal-mode fix: buildSessionInvocation was wrapping the prompt with `codex exec --dangerously-bypass… <prompt>`, which is the HEADLESS one-shot subcommand — so picking "terminal mode" for Codex actually ran the non-interactive flow piped through a PTY (the "regular Codex" UX the user saw). Now launches the interactive TUI (`codex`, no subcommand) with initialPrompt pasted after ready timer, and resumes via `codex resume <session-id>`.

[2026-04-20] AgentIdentity avatar branch now uses `flex` + `rounded-md` to match the icon branch. Chips with `preferredAgents` are filtered out of `visibleActions` when none of their preferred dispatchers exist in `agents` — so trimmed installs never see a delegation chip that would silently route to a non-dispatcher. [2026-05-14] Fixed dashboard navbar tabs disappearing on narrow viewports. Root cause: header used display:flex with no flex-wrap, and .tabs container/its buttons had no flex-shrink protection — when h1 + 5 tabs + 'Last updated' text exceeded viewport width, flex compressed the tab buttons until their text and borders got clipped off the right edge. Fix: header { flex-wrap: wrap; gap: 12px 16px; }, h1 + .last get flex-shrink: 0 + white-space: nowrap, .tabs { flex-wrap: wrap; min-width: 0; }, .tab { flex-shrink: 0; white-space: nowrap; }. Now tabs wrap to a second row on narrow viewports instead of disappearing. Deployed worker version 6ac5c07c-93ad-4a68-8d4d-db7ce45e810f.
[2026-05-14] Fixed sidebar tree indentation collapsing in RTL: tree-node row used inline paddingLeft and left: positions which always anchor to physical left regardless of dir, so RTL items all sat flush at the right edge. Switched to logical properties (paddingInlineStart, insetInlineStart, end-, start-, text-start, rounded-e-, ms-auto) so depth-16px indent now flips to the right edge in RTL.
[2026-05-16] Wired OpenCode dynamic model discovery end-to-end (fixes recurring Discord reports: users with Minimax/GLM/Kimi/Zen saw only the hardcoded OpenAI/Anthropic/Google/XAI fallback). Root cause was two coupled bugs: the listModels() endpoint shipped earlier had zero frontend consumers, and resolveProviderModel resolved only against the static list so saved opencode/* selections were silently snapped to models[0]. Providers API now advertises dynamicModels; new app-store ensureProviderModels() lazily hydrates the real entitlement-gated list (opencode models = authed providers + Zen free subset, verified live = 97 ids); GET .../models?refresh=1 busts the 60s cache; resolveProviderModel preserves an unknown saved id while un-hydrated; a searchable sub-provider-grouped combobox replaces the matrix for dynamic providers (Pi fixed for free). Extracted pure parseOpenCodeModels; added 10 unit tests. PROVIDER-CLI.md §12.1 #3 corrected (was a phantom) + migration entry #22.
[2026-05-16] Made the OpenCode dynamic-discovery fix generic across providers. Audited all 8 — only opencode + pi implement listModels(); the capability-driven wiring (provider.dynamicModels) already covers both. Pi had the identical latent bug (pi --list-models output that is non-empty but all-#-banner returned [] → blank picker), so applied the same hardening: extracted pure parsePiModels with the empty/banner-only → offline-fallback guard + 15s timeout, mirroring parseOpenCodeModels. Added test/pi-models-parse.test.ts (16/16 model-discovery tests pass). PROVIDER-CLI.md updated: §11 #22 + §12.1 #3 corrected (Pi was not "fixed for free"), §9 lists the new tests, §13 gained a "Dynamic model discovery (capability-driven)" contract so future listModels providers get the combobox/hydration/guard with zero component edits.
[2026-05-16] OpenCode seamless-integration follow-up (A+C+B). A: auth-aware healthCheck — parses `opencode auth list` (pure parseOpenCodeAuth, ANSI-stripped) so the readiness text is honest ("· 2 providers configured" vs "· no provider keys — Zen free models only") while keeping authenticated:true (Zen -free needs no key; flipping it would hide OpenCode from the composer). C: listModels() now throws on genuine CLI failure so the models route's `dynamic` flag is honest; dynamic returned on cache hits; app-store gates modelsHydrated on dynamic; combobox shows an amber "offline defaults — configure + Refresh" hint when dynamic:false. B: new optional AgentProvider.buildVerifyCommand(defaultModel) — verify route injects the Cabinet default model only when that provider is the configured default, so "verify passed" tests the real path. OpenCode+Pi only (6 others untouched). Tests 26/26, tsc/lint clean. PROVIDER-CLI.md §6 + migration #23.
[2026-05-17] Fixed "Failed to fetch" runtime error overlay crashing the tasks board and Skill Library. Both had an async refresh useCallback with try/finally but no catch, invoked from useEffect (and void refresh()/SSE/focus) without a catch — so a transient fetch rejection (offline, dev HMR dropping an in-flight request, daemon restart) bubbled to the Next error overlay instead of degrading. Wrapped refreshOverview + refreshConversations (use-board-data.ts) and refresh (skill-library.tsx) in try/catch that keeps last-known state and console.warns. Endpoints verified reachable (not a broken route); this is resilience for background refreshes and helps real users on network blips too.
[2026-05-17] Localized the entire app into 11 new languages (15 total). Added scripts/i18n-translate.mjs — a resumable, placeholder-safe Gemini JSON-mode batch translator (gemini-2.5-flash, GOOGLE_AI_API_KEY from .cabinet.env) that flattens en.json's 1120 leaf strings, translates in concurrent batches of 48, verifies {{interpolation}}/<n> tag/brand integrity per batch with retry+backoff, and rebuilds each locale in en.json's exact key order; exposed as `npm run i18n:translate`. Generated hi/es/fr/ar/bn/pt/ru/ur/id/de/ja.json (1120/1120 each, 0 missing, 0 placeholder loss). Wired all 11 into src/i18n/index.ts (SUPPORTED_LOCALES, LOCALE_LABELS native names, resources), formatters.ts (LOCALE_TO_BCP47), and removed them from REQUESTABLE_LOCALES. settings-page LanguageSection now derives the picker from SUPPORTED_LOCALES+LOCALE_LABELS so future locales surface automatically. ar/ur inherit existing RTL_LOCALE_PREFIXES. All four registries aligned (15==15==15==15), tsc/eslint clean for touched files.

[2026-05-23] Fix: onboarding starter-task placeholder (and home greeting) showed the OS username ("Hi, I'm <os-username>!") instead of the name typed in onboarding. Root cause: app-shell reads the user profile during the wizard, before onboarding writes workspace.json, so profile-io seedProfileFromOnboarding() fell back to os.userInfo().username AND persisted it to user.json; onboarding never wrote the entered name, so the OS value stuck. Fix: (1) /api/onboarding/setup now writes user.json with answers.name; (2) readUserProfile only persists a seeded profile when the name came from onboarding (workspace home name) - a pure OS-username fallback stays transient so it can be corrected. tsc clean.

[2026-05-23] Fix: running a task failed + task page failed to load. Multiple rooms-v3 regressions found via a real run ("convert this onboarding video to webm" mentioning a 74MB onboarding.mov): (1) ROOT: buildMentionContext (conversation-runner) inlined the mentioned file's raw bytes into the prompt — a 74MB .mov became a 134MB prompt.md, which failed the run and made the conversation API return ~134MB so the task page choked. Now binary/large mentions (video/audio/image/pdf/office/archive by extension) are referenced by path ("open with the Read tool") instead of inlined, and inlined text is capped at 200KB. (2) Task dispatched to "editor" which didn't exist — onboarding only created the user's first agent (ceo). onboarding/setup now always instantiates the canonical "editor" agent; also added editor to the existing sales room. (3) TaskConversationPage fetched the task with no cabinetPath (chicken-and-egg) so it couldn't find the room's conversation -> "fails to load"; now app-shell passes section.cabinetPath and the initial fetchTask uses it. (4) The recent-tasks rail fetched conversations + agent roster unscoped (empty home after rooms-v3); now scoped to the active room. Deleted the broken 134MB conversation. tsc clean.

[2026-05-23] Fix: top-level rooms showed a "Back" button that navigated up into the neutral home container ("Jane's Home" / data-dir root) — you should always be inside a room, never the dir above. tree-view: the Back button (and openParentCabinet) is now hidden/guarded when the parent cabinet is the home root (parentIsHome = parentCabinet.path === "."), so it only appears for genuinely nested sub-cabinets within a room. Defensive: app-shell's landing redirect now also snaps ANY content section scoped to "." (home container) into the default room, not just the bare home screen — so the app can never sit on the dir above a room. tsc clean.

[2026-05-23] Auto-refresh the sidebar tree when a conversation creates artifacts. app-shell now subscribes to the global conversation event stream (/api/agents/conversations/events) and, on a task.updated whose payload.artifactPaths is non-empty, reloads the tree (debounced 400ms) so agent-created/modified files appear without a manual refresh. [2026-06-07] Implemented the Schedule Calendar PRD (Phases 0-4). [2026-06-08] Implemented Schedule Calendar PRD Phase 5 item "this and following" (recurrence series split). Dragging a recurring occurrence now offers a third choice between "This occurrence" and "All events": cap the original series at the split instant and fork a new recurring series from there with the dropped cadence. Mechanism is a symmetric series window — added `since`/`until` (iCalendar DTSTART/UNTIL) to JobConfig + CabinetJobSummary, mapped in normalizeJob/normalizeJobConfig (conditional-spread like exceptions); a recurring job emits no occurrences before `since` (inclusive) or at/after `until` (exclusive). BOTH bounds are required for correctness: capping the original with `until` alone would let the forked daily cadence "leak" backward onto days before the split and double-book them, so the fork carries `since`. getScheduleEvents filters the window (early `until` break since occurrences are monotonic; `since` skip); the shared `withinSeriesWindow(job, when)` helper in one-off.ts is the single source of truth, reused server-side. node-cron has no end-date, so the jobs run handler enforces the window server-side (like EXDATE): out-of-window scheduler fires return `skipped: series-window`, and a fully-ended capped series (its `until` now past) is retired inline (enabled:false + reload) so the daemon stops firing the zombie cron daily. schedule-view performMove gained a "following" scope (optimistic `until` patch on the original + POST a `since`-bounded fork with explicit unique id, rollback on failure); reconcile + jobConfigToSummary now carry since/until; MoveConfirmDialog shows the third option. New test/cron-compute-series-window.test.ts (6 cases: until exclusive, since inclusive, open bounds, capped-before-split, no-backward-leak vs unbounded control, clean week partition). tsc + eslint clean; new + existing cron-compute tests pass. In-browser drag verification still pending. PRD updated.

[2026-06-15] Scheduler daemon now authenticates its server-to-server triggers (jobs, one-shot disable, heartbeats) against the KB_PASSWORD gate via authCookieHeader() in the shared PBKDF2 kb-auth module. Fixes silent 401s that disabled all scheduled runs whenever KB_PASSWORD was set (supersedes #137, builds on #140's PBKDF2 hardening; merged as #142). Follow-up: generalized the daemon's .env backfill to all three auth inputs (KB_PASSWORD + CABINET_AUTH_SALT + CABINET_LOGIN_PBKDF2_ITERS) so an override set only in .env can't desync the prod start:daemon path; refreshed docs/AUTH.md (daemon S2S is done, not "separate"); added authCookieHeader unit test + an end-to-end proxy.test.ts guard that the daemon's cookie passes the real proxy() gate.
